Exports Suffer a Major Blow

(Tokyo) Although the U.S. ban on gold exports was not entirely unexpected, it has caused widespread anxiety in Japan, fearing that the result will be an appreciation of the Japanese yen, which will severely hit the silk industry and affect farmers and businesses. Exports of electrical appliances, rubber shoes, and groceries will also inevitably suffer. However, optimists believe that although the Japanese yen will appreciate, it will not exceed 25 U.S. cents, so there is no reason for excessive pessimism. (6th Reuters)

(Tokyo) The impact of the U.S. financial panic on Japan is more serious than leaving the League of Nations. Exchanges across the country have uniformly closed for two days, and the silk market has closed for four days. At the same time, the Ministries of Commerce and Industry, Agriculture and Forestry, Foreign Affairs, and Finance have all convened ministerial meetings to discuss countermeasures closely. Japanese Finance Minister Takahashi Korekiyo invited Bank of Japan Governor Hisashi Hijikata and Yokohama Specie Bank President Kenji Kodama to the ministry to participate in the discussion. Financial circles are deeply concerned that the U.S. panic will ruin the Japanese exchange rate market and trigger a domestic agricultural panic. It is rumored that the result of the meeting of key financial figures is that if the U.S. ban on gold exports becomes a practical implementation, Japan's foreign trade will be most severely affected. Foreign yarns, white sugar, and various commodities will be imported in large quantities, and Japanese industry will inevitably be pressured. To prevent the inflow of foreign goods and coordinate foreign trade, the Japanese government must promptly use exchange rate management laws to prevent the appreciation of the Japanese yen. On the one hand, it should raise tariffs to prevent the inflow of foreign goods into Japan. (6th China United Press dispatch)

(Tokyo) The Central Japan Silk Industry Association convened a joint meeting today. Irie, Director of the Sericulture Department of the Ministry of Agriculture and Forestry, and others attended the meeting to discuss countermeasures to deal with the U.S. financial panic. Japan's exports to the United States in 1932 totaled 444,514,700 yuan, of which silk accounted for 306,014,900 yuan, or 80 percent. Once the U.S.-Japan exchange rate changes, Japanese farmers will fall back into a tragic hell. Therefore, the Japanese Ministry of Agriculture and Forestry is particularly concerned about the future of the U.S. panic and is working closely with trade associations to study countermeasures. Currently, because the United States itself has not yet made a decision, Japan naturally cannot decide on countermeasures in advance. (6th China United Press)

Dai Chuanxian Speaks on the Japanese Aggressive Ambitions 36

At the National Government Memorial Week

Recalling Impressions of a Small Banquet During His Trip to Japan

(Nanjing) The National Government held a memorial week at 9 a.m. on the 6th. Yu Youren, Dai Chuanxian, Niu Yongjian, Jing Hengyi, Zhou Zhenlin, Zhu Jiahua, Wang Yongbin, Chen Shuren, Liang Hancao, Chen Shaokuan, He Yaozu, Huang Musong, Chen Yi, Lu Chao, Wei Huai, and more than 500 National Government staff members attended. Chairman Lin led the ceremony. Dai Chuanxian reported, stating that the recent resolution of the League of Nations has made it clear that Japan is invading us and that right and wrong have been clearly distinguished by the world. However, Japan has been attacking with increasing ferocity in the past two weeks. From before the September 18th Incident until now, the Japanese clearly know that their actions are illegal and violate justice, but they still act recklessly. If a determination on legality and justice could make Japan realize its errors, there would not be today. I remember in 1927, I was ordered to go to Japan and stayed in Tokyo for more than 60 days, giving more than 80 public speeches. After each speech, I debated with the audience and eventually made most of the anti-Japanese people deeply understand that our party and our ideas were very legitimate and deeply admired them. When I was about to leave Japan, I heard that the Revolutionary Army had recovered Nanjing, and at this time, the Japanese military authorities suddenly invited me to a banquet. During the banquet, the host gave a toast, saying that he greatly admired Mr.'s advocacy and the Kuomintang's principles. Now that your country's revolutionary regime has been placed on the international stage, there is still one thing to say: the prosperity of a country does not depend on talking but on having the strength to do it. Japan's achievements today are entirely due to what it has done. Please drink a glass to wish you hard work and so on. The tone and demeanor were extremely ferocious and cold. This feeling and impression have never been forgotten by me. At that time, their performance had already foreshadowed the fact that they would invade our country today. Now, the whole world has made it clear who is right and wrong in Japan's invasion of us. If we want this judgment to be effective, only the Chinese themselves can make thorough efforts to achieve this goal. Especially in the last two weeks, we have suffered such violence. It is not good for me to say anything, so I bring up the impression of the small banquet in Japan at that time to let you know the intentions of the Japanese and their views on right and wrong, based on their own responsibilities and their future path, which are very clear. I hope that you comrades will be vigilant. The ceremony ended at 10 o'clock. (6th Special Dispatch)

Foreign Minister Luo's Speech at the Ministry of Foreign Affairs Memorial Week 37

Denies Rumors of Resigning Due to Illness

Encourages Colleagues to Persevere and Endure Hardship

(Nanjing) On the morning of the 6th, at the Ministry of Foreign Affairs Memorial Week, Minister Luo made the following remarks on the Rehe incident: I have been at the ministry since January 28th of last year, and it has been a year since then. I am grateful to my colleagues for their assistance and hard work. It is undeniable that the recent military setbacks have affected diplomacy. From now on, those who handle diplomacy should not blame fate or others, but should raise their spirits and fight to the end. The difficulties ahead may be greater than the present or greater than the past few decades. However, the more difficulties there are, the more we must fight. The Rehe incident should be observed as a normal event, not as an accident, and we should not be discouraged. How to recover lost territory depends on how we fight. A Shanghai newspaper on the 5th reported that "Luo Wengan resigned due to illness," which is purely a rumor and absolutely untrue. Today, I read in the Jingbao newspaper that "Foreign Minister Luo is in pain and wants to die." Pain and anger are certainly present, but the desire to die is not. It is possible to be killed by the enemy, but it is impossible to die of illness. There is illness, but no claiming to be ill. I will certainly resign when times are comfortable, but I will not resign when times are difficult. No matter how difficult the situation is, I am determined to do my best. The more difficult things are, the more they must be done. I hope my colleagues will work hard, persevere, and endure hardship for ten or several decades. The failure of the Rehe incident this time is mostly due to the hearts of the people. Colleagues must change this atmosphere and abide by the ancient saying "Give my all until my heart stops beating" and work hard. (6th Central News Agency dispatch)

Central Party Headquarters Held Memorial Week Yesterday 41

Dai Chuanxian's Report

National Revival Depends Entirely on Struggle

In the past, we hoped that the League of Nations would take action, but as a result, although it failed to achieve actual sanctions, right and wrong have been clarified. This shows that justice and fairness have not been extinguished. However, whether justice can ultimately prevail still depends on solving the problem of our own efforts. We must rely on our own struggle. Only by following the Prime Minister's last words, "If you cannot succeed, you must become benevolent," can we save the country from danger. Those in the battlefield should be like this, and comrades in the rear and the people of the whole country should also embrace this spirit and maximize their abilities in their duties or professions to actively assist us. If we cannot do this, even if the League of Nations can uphold justice, it cannot turn our country's critical situation into safety. Hardship revitalizes the nation, which has been proven by historical facts. We cannot estimate the time of our national salvation efforts. Perhaps it will take months or perhaps years. Beiping and Tianjin Markets are Cold and Desolate 42

Dongjiaomin Lane Becomes Bustling Again

(Beiping) After the fall of Chengde, the city of Beiping was shaken, and merchants and residents were saddened and uneasy. The market was immediately cold and desolate. Dongjiaomin Lane became bustling again. Wealthy merchants moved valuable items and moved to hotels in the lane in an endless stream. The Security Zone Management Committee held a meeting today to discuss measures to maintain public order. (6th Special Dispatch)

(Tianjin) Customs reports that recently, merchant ships traveling to and from Tianjin and Shanghai have either turned back midway or temporarily suspended navigation due to the loss of Rehe. Merchants from southern provinces sitting in Tianjin have also ended their business and gone south, and transactions have completely stopped. (6th Special Dispatch)

(Beiping) The 3,000 rickshaws that were hired to transport supplies to the Gubeikou and Miyun areas were caught in the fall of Chengde. Refugees from outside the pass returned to the area to escape, and women and children competed to hire rickshaws. Supply could not meet demand, and they raised prices sharply, earning ten times the profit and returning fully loaded. (6th Special Dispatch)

German General Election Results: Government Party Achieves Unprecedented Victory 81

Occupies Absolute Majority of 647 Seats in Parliament

Breaks Pivotal Position of Catholic Centre Party

Hitler's Arduous Struggle Finally Succeeds

Expected that Anti-Red Movement Will Become More Severe in the Future

Reuters, Berlin, 6th The election was a great victory for Hitler, and the methods he used have worked. The people mostly trust him. The National Socialists now not only occupy 288 seats in parliament, but also with the assistance of the two right-wing parties, namely the German National People's Party and the German People's Party, they can obtain a majority of about 23 seats in parliament, thereby breaking the long-standing deadlock in parliament.

Reuters, Berlin, 6th According to the official report released by the Electoral Commission today, with the help of the National People's Party and the German People's Party, the National Socialist Party will have a majority of 47 seats in the new parliament. The new parliament has a total of 647 seats. The National Socialist Party occupies 288 seats, the National People's Party occupies 52 seats, and the German People's Party occupies 7 seats, for a total of 347 seats. Those who oppose Hitler, namely the Socialist Party and the National Party, occupy 125 seats, the Communist Party 81 seats, the Centre Party 73 seats, the Bavarian People's Party 19 seats, plus another 2 seats, for a total of 300 seats.

National, Berlin, 6th It can be said that the German parliament has entered a new era today. The government has gained the support of the majority of the country and can now consolidate its position and implement administrative and constitutional changes, which are necessary to begin its national policy. The first effect of Sunday's development will likely be that the government's anti-red movement will be even more severe than before in order to eradicate the communist scourge. This is one of the goals announced by Hitler. Hitler has become a national hero today. Tracing back to the beginning of his rise, the people of the country all laughed at his foolishness, but Hitler was not deterred by it. Relying on his inner self and perseverance, he promoted his doctrine, and first had hundreds of followers, then increased to thousands, then tens of thousands, then hundreds of thousands and millions. He exhausted himself and tasted hardships. After thirteen years of thorns, he finally reached Kangzhuang and became the leader of 70 million people, holding the key to the gate of saving the country. It can be said that where there is a will, there is a way.

Havas, Berlin, 6th Goering, the Minister of the Interior of Prussia, issued a notice, saying that "[yesterday, the nationalist front achieved a great advantage. Since the Bismarck era, the Centre Party has always occupied a pivotal position in the political situation, but now it has been destroyed. This is really the first time. In addition, it is noteworthy that in the southern states, the National Socialist Party has an even greater advantage. Therefore, the governments of the southern states have no right to continue to represent public opinion to govern the states, because public opinion has already attached itself to Hitler," etc. This is probably the first declaration issued by the leaders of the National Socialist Party after the election, which was directed at the governments of the southern states, with the intention of advising the governments of the states to find ways to adapt to the policies adopted by the federal government and Prussia in politics.

Comparison of Votes of Various Parties 82

Reuters, Berlin, 6th According to the officially announced number of votes cast yesterday, the total was 39,289,854 votes, so the new parliament will have 642 seats, which is really the most populous parliament in German history. The National Socialist Party ranked first in the number of votes, with 17,244,323 votes, followed by the Socialist Party with 7,176,226 votes, followed by the Communist Party with 4,746,034 votes, followed by the Centre Party with 4,289,354 votes, followed by the German National People's Party with 3,131,336 votes, followed by the Bavarian People's Party with 1,206,293 votes. The German People's Party, the Christian Social Party, and the German National Party all received less than 500,000 votes.

Results of the Prussian Parliament Re-election 83

Havas, Berlin, 6th The Prussian State Assembly elected yesterday has approximately 470 members, and the distribution of each party is as follows: 207 seats for the National Socialist Party, 79 seats for the Social Democratic Party, 63 seats for the Communist Party, 67 seats for the Centre Party, 43 seats for the National People's Party, and 3 seats for the Democratic Party. The parties belonging to the government side have a total of 250 seats.

National Socialist Party Issues Proclamation 84

Havas, Berlin, 6th The National Socialist Party Information Office issued a notice, saying that the victory won by the party in the federal lower house election and the Prussian state assembly election is extremely important. The German people's trust in the process of great national construction has been clearly proven here. If the National Socialist Party movement and its heroic struggle had not rescued Germany from the abyss, then Germany would have already fallen into poverty and could not survive today. The notice concludes, "The National Socialist Party now has the right to carry out the nation's verdict against Marxism, and at the same time, it is even more powerful to revive Germany and lead Germany to a better future."

No Changes in Cabinet Organization 85

New Parliament to Convene on April 1st

National, Berlin, 6th The Cabinet issued a declaration today, saying that the great victory in this election is due to the Prime Minister's unyielding spirit. The current organization of the government will not be changed because of this. After the necessary formalities are completed, the Parliament will be convened as soon as possible within this month.

National, Berlin, 6th It was officially announced today that the German Parliament is scheduled to convene on April 1st in the Potsdam Garrison Church.

A List of Elected Leaders 86

Berlin, 6th (Havas Dispatch) - The following are the elected officials of the major political parties in the House of Representatives election: (1) From the National Socialist Party: Prime Minister Hitler (his first time entering Parliament), Federal Interior Minister Frick, Prussian Interior Minister Göring, Prince August Wilhelm (grandson of the deposed Emperor Wilhelm), and Count Bismarck (descendant of the Iron Chancellor). (2) From the German National People's Party: current Federal Minister of Economics and Food Hugenberg, Federal Vice-Chancellor von Papen, and Labor Minister Seldte. (3) From the Social Democratic Party: Prime Minister Braun of the Prussian constitutional government (Braun is Hitler's sworn enemy), former Speaker of the House of Representatives Löbe, and former Prussian Interior Minister Severing. (4) From the Centre Party: former Prime Minister Brüning, Party leader Prelate Kaas, and former Federal Labor Minister Stegerwald. (5) From the Communist Party: party leader Thälmann and Ms. Zetkin (who is 76 years old and was first elected to Parliament in 1920).

Enthusiastic Participation in Voting 87

Stormtroopers' Armed Parade - Berlin Resembles Wartime State - Berlin, 5th (Havas Dispatch) - Today's House of Representatives election saw a large number of voters. The weather was fine, so voters were very enthusiastic. Until 4:00 PM, no major incidents occurred. The atmosphere was calm in the morning, but became tense in the afternoon. The main streets in and around central Berlin were thronged with people, making Berlin resemble a city occupied by troops. This was because the Nazi stormtroopers and Stahlhelm members were parading everywhere in uniform. 35,000 Stahlhelm members gathered in southwestern Berlin and marched from the Brandenburg Gate to Unter den Linden in central Berlin until 4:00 PM. The sidewalks on both sides were packed with people. The flags carried by the various private armies were similar to the military flags of the imperial era. When these flags passed, the crowd sang the national anthem, and the people followed the Stahlhelm troops with great interest. In general, the Stahlhelm party was more prevalent in the center of Berlin. They appeared to not carry weapons. In the areas surrounding the city, the Nazi stormtroopers were more numerous. Since this morning, the Nazi troops have been converging on Berlin from various locations by train or truck. Many of them wore armbands with the words "Auxiliary Police" and patrolled everywhere with pistols and batons. Even Nazi troops who were not part of the auxiliary police carried pistols or weapons. The Nazi troops used police express trucks used by the police. The police cars have been under their free control. The Nazi troops had gathered near Berlin beforehand and only arrived in the city today. The entire police force was mobilized, carrying pistols, rifles, and machine guns while patrolling the streets. Cars equipped with extremely powerful searchlights accompanied them.

Berlin, 5th (Havas Dispatch) - During the German election, German expatriates residing abroad participated in voting for the first time today. Germans abroad were issued permits by the German consul in their location and traveled to the nearest German locality to vote. German authorities organized special transportation in the border areas to facilitate these expatriates. 15 to 20 percent of German expatriates residing in Czechoslovakia have already voted. Many German expatriates in Vienna, Tyrol, and eastern Austria have also returned to vote. It is estimated that more than 10,000 people have returned from Denmark to vote.

The Left and Right are Irreconcilable 88

Berlin, 6th (Reuters) - The National Socialist Party is unusually jubilant about the victory in this election. It is widely expected that the National Socialist Party may arrest all communist members so that they do not have to rely on the assistance of friendly parties and can hold an overwhelming majority in Parliament. The National Socialist Party is still pursuing its policy of eliminating political enemies. All newspapers of the Socialist Party in Thuringia have been banned from publication twice. The power of the Socialist mayor to manage police affairs has been stripped. Furthermore, the General Association of German Jews in Thuringia has been disbanded. The National Socialist Party has taken over the police administration of the Free City of Hamburg by order of Interior Minister Dr. Frick because an anti-National Socialist coalition holds power there.

Hamburg Falls into Nazi Hands 89

Hamburg, 5th (Havas Agency) - The Free City of Hamburg has, until now, held an opposing attitude towards the National Socialist Party. Tonight, the National Socialist Party forcibly seized the administrative power of the city. Two to three hundred Nazi stormtroopers entered the city government around 10 PM and occupied it. The Nazi party leader in Hamburg, Gauleiter Kaufmann, gave a short speech on the balcony of the city government. Other party leaders were also present at the scene. Federal Interior Minister Frick ordered the local police to immediately hand over the administrative power of the Free City to Senator Liesche, a member of the Nazi Party and a member of the Hamburg Senate. Although the Hamburg Senate protested, they had no choice but to obey in fact. Mayor Petersen has already resigned. The city government was surrounded by National Socialist organizations, and some civilians participated, singing the German national anthem and the Nazi Party song.

The Election Situation is Still Stable 90

Berlin, 6th (National News) - The general election situation was generally stable. However, small-scale conflicts occurred in Worms and Darmstadt, where six people were injured. In Breslau, many communists rioted and fought, resulting in the death of one policeman and another officer seriously injured. Later, the police arrested about 100 communists.

George Bernard Shaw Arrives in Yokohama 91

Tokyo, 6th (Reuters) - George Bernard Shaw arrived in Yokohama this morning and, with his humorous attitude, told reporters, "The crisis in the American banking industry is the best thing that could happen. Any country that allows banks to be run by private individuals should suffer such a blow." Shaw visited Tokyo today and returned to Yokohama in the afternoon.

Chicago Mayor Dies of Serious Injuries 92

Miami, 6th (Reuters) - Chicago Mayor Cermak, who was shot in the abdomen on the 16th of this month when someone attempted to assassinate President Roosevelt, died today due to ineffective treatment at the age of 59. Cermak was born near Prague, and moved to the United States when he was just one year old. From the age of twelve, he worked in factories and mines while studying at night school. Later he studied law and eventually became a judge. In 1931, he was elected mayor of Chicago and was renowned for clearing up long-standing abuses and severely punishing local tyrants. The criminal Zangara has been sentenced to 80 years in prison. Now that Cermak is dead, the criminal will be charged with murder, which will result in the death penalty.

Chaos in Northern Manchuria Under the Iron Heel of the Japanese Army 93

Songhua River Puppet Army Defects and Resists Japan

Gambling dens abound along the Chinese Eastern Railway

British goods entering Manchuria are all excluded

Harbin, 25th (Special Correspondence of the North-China Daily News) - In the past two weeks, the Japanese army has been frequently mobilizing in the Songhua River area. Before the 14th, 700 people had been traveling down the river in long-distance buses. It is now known that the leading scout car, which was about 500 yards ahead of the main convoy, carried ten Japanese soldiers, one White Russian driver, and one assistant. It was supposed to stop at a location 40 miles from Sanxing Gorge (near Yilan), but suddenly disappeared. The area is located at a river bend and has a high hill. When the main convoy passed, guns fired from the hill, causing many Japanese soldiers to be killed or injured. Seven cars were then used to carry the wounded back to Harbin. The cars were too badly damaged to be used again. Three days ago, the Japanese military authorities again requisitioned 20 long-distance buses to transport troops downstream, but the Chinese and Russian drivers refused to drive. The Japanese army then intercepted 20 long-distance buses on the street, expelled the passengers, and forced them to drive downstream. Two of the drivers, realizing the purpose of the requisition, jumped off and escaped. The Japanese then ordered the company to find replacements. The company could not comply and excused itself by saying that it could not find reliable drivers. No one knows what the true situation is downstream of the Songhua River. It is said that the troops of the "Manchukuo" in Fujin and along the river have mostly defected and joined the anti-Manchu army because there are still many armed forces resisting "Manchukuo" in that area. Another report claims that 432 Japanese expatriates who went to develop the lower reaches of the Songhua River last year were attacked by anti-Manchu troops. Japanese troops from Harbin were dispatched to protect the Japanese expatriates. However, regardless of the truth of either statement, this situation shows that there is no peace and order in many areas of northern Manchuria. Furthermore, since the original Japanese troops stationed there have been moving south in large numbers in the past few days, there may soon be more anti-Manchu battles. Currently, vehicles coming east along the Chinese Eastern Railway are often filled with refugees from the border areas. Passenger cars that can carry 40 people often carry as many as 85. This shows that the Chinese people in the area anticipate war soon and are fleeing in large numbers. This is another evidence of the unrest in eastern Jilin. In the past, the Harbin authorities could boast of strictly enforcing the ban on gambling. If a gambling den was discovered, the police would immediately seal it off and severely punish the owners. Now, however, gambling dens abound in Chuandian and the major cities and towns along the Chinese Eastern Railway, sucking up the people's money. These gambling dens have special areas for people of all three social classes. There are even places set up specifically for rickshaw pullers to gamble with a few copper coins. Most of the gambling den owners are White Russians. It is said that there are currently more than 500 gambling dens in the Chuandian district alone. They often set up gambling dens in public places and gamble openly. According to a Western newspaper, the authorities collect gambling taxes, ranging from 200 to 1,000 yuan per month per establishment. They are also closely monitored, and the tax amount is increased as soon as their income increases. At present, larger cities and towns along the Chinese Eastern Railway, such as Anda, Ang'angxi, Hailar, and Manchuria, are all covered in gambling dens. It is no wonder that the number of people committing suicide is increasing day by day, there are groups of beggars on the streets, and robbery cases occur every day. The "Manchukuo" customs often create difficulties for foreign imports by unreasonably levying taxes. Recently, a batch of pure British wool fabrics arrived in Dalian, and the customs officers forcibly claimed that the goods contained 2% artificial silk, imposing a heavy tax of 45% ad valorem. These goods had been frequently transported to Manchuria in the previous five years, and their quality was sufficient to prevent rain. It is ridiculous that the Japanese claimed that they contained artificial silk. Therefore, it can be considered that the Japanese want to block the import of British goods. In addition, incidents of obstructing foreign trade are even more frequent. The Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs has repeatedly stated that Manchuria is open. Now, its door is obviously only open to those going to Manchuria, but it is not easy for those coming to Manchuria to enter the country. In the past, British insurance companies did well in Manchuria, but now not only must all government offices insure with Japanese insurance companies, but those who insure with European insurance companies will also be regarded as spies, and their property may be confiscated. In short, in any industry that the Japanese can operate, they exclude Westerners. Foreigners in Manchuria can only sell goods that the Japanese cannot counterfeit.

The Japanese Consul in Tianjin Protests Unreasonably 94

Muzzling Claiming That Stationing Troops in Muzhuangzi Violates the Treaty

The Provincial Government Did Not Reply Because It Was Not a Fact

The Boxer Protocol Should Be Mutually Observed

Tianjin Correspondence - The Japanese Consul General in Tianjin, Kazue Kuwashima, recently claimed that Chinese troops were stationed in Muzhuangzi, violating the Boxer Protocol's stipulation that "no troops are allowed within 20 li of Tianjin." He protested to the Hebei Provincial Government a few days ago. The Provincial Government did not reply, believing that the Consul's claims were completely untrue. Yesterday, Chairman Yu of the Provincial Government stated that Japan often invokes the Boxer Protocol to restrict our activities, but does not know that this treaty does not only concern China and Japan, and the obligation to abide by it is a responsibility that all parties concerned should jointly bear. Even the Japanese army's occupation of Yuguan has violated the dignity of the treaty, but they are still sophistical and evasive. Recently, they have made three consecutive protests to our Provincial Government. The reason for the first protest was to oppose the deployment of our troops. The excuse for the second protest was that our troops were building forts in Dagu. The third protest was the so-called stationing of troops in Muzhuangzi. The first two protests have been replied to, as they were all based on misunderstandings and relied on the Boxer Protocol to make demands. The claim that forts are being built at Dagu is completely inaccurate and can be easily proven by the facts. Digging trenches is only a temporary exercise and does not conflict with any of the provisions of the treaty. As for the Japanese army in Tianjin's previous statement that it will jointly supervise the Chinese local government to fulfill its obligations with the consuls of the other Boxer Protocol signatory countries, namely Britain, France, and Italy, the Provincial Government has not officially heard of this matter. However, it is confident that the Chinese government is always abiding by the treaty, but it also hopes that the relevant countries will exercise their power in case of emergency and impose severe sanctions on those who violate the treaty. Furthermore, more than 100 Japanese soldiers who invaded Rehe have been transported back to the rear for treatment due to frostbite. The Japanese military authorities have publicized that this was caused by a poisonous gas attack by the Chinese army, which is purely to confuse international public opinion. "Frostbite" and "poisoning" can be distinguished by their symptoms. Since the Japanese have created this atmosphere, it is important to pay attention to whether they intend to use poisonous gas to attack the Rehe army. (March 4)

Songjiang 95

Xifengjia Village, Eighth District, Robbed

Two Bandit Boats Discovered in the River off Xujiaqiao, Xiaokunshan Last Night - The villagers of Da Lou Township, who first discovered the bandit boats, sounded the gongs to alert others. The neighboring villages followed suit, and the sound of the gongs filled the sky. The bandits did not dare to act and fled west. However, more than ten bandits landed in Xifengjia Village, within the territory of Tianma Mountain. Carrying two pistols and speaking in a mix of local dialects, they rushed into the Zhao family to rob. However, the villagers of the village had heard that Xiaokunshan had been robbed many times and were prepared. Every night, someone patrolled. When the bandits were robbing in the Zhao family's house, they were suddenly startled by the villagers sounding the gongs and shouting to catch them. They fled west. Fortunately, the Zhao family did not suffer any losses.

Wuxi 96

Construction of the Xijing Road

Feng Junyan, Chief of the Sixth District, and Zhao Yingqiu, Chief of the Seventh District, are raising large sums of money to build the Xijing Road for the sake of facilitating transportation. The road starts from the Tangtou Bashiqiao in Dongbeitang and ends at Zhangjingqiao, with a total length of 14 miles. The original road was narrow and unusable, and it is now planned to be widened to nine feet. The entire road project requires approximately 14,000 workers. The former Construction Bureau has already sent personnel to the countryside to survey the road and mark it with lime. Construction was originally scheduled to begin on the first of this month, but the project has been delayed until now due to continuous cloudy and rainy weather. Construction will begin as soon as the weather clears and warms. All construction procedures have been prepared.

Nantong 98

Bandits Repelled at Guanyintang

A large group of bandits gathered and rioted in Guanyintang, in the east of this county. On the 4th, more than 100 bandits fired on the security corps in the Jinle and Xiting districts. The police corps of neighboring districts also rushed to assist in the suppression. The bandits, unable to resist, retreated towards Er Dongdu. While pursuing them, on the 5th, the county government dispatched guerrillas to intercept them.

Magistrate Zhang has requested the Fourth District to hand over Chen Yide, and has immediately transferred him to the court for trial according to the law.

Changzhou 100

Opening a Coffin for Autopsy in a Private Murder Case - Jiang Cairong, a villager from Liuducun near Liyuncun in the Ninth District of Wuyi County, injured and killed Shen Yinbao, a beggar, during a wax sacrifice last year. Jiang Cairong was released on bail by the Eighth Sub-bureau of Public Security and privately settled the case without reporting it. Yang Kongyi, the chief prosecutor of the county court, heard about the incident and went to the countryside to open the coffin for autopsy the day before yesterday. That night, he stayed in the Yunxun Village Inn and interrogated Shen Chen, the mother of the deceased, and Miao Nuying, the village chief, as well as Ma Jusheng and others who mediated the private settlement. Shen Chen and others requested that the coffin not be opened for autopsy. The village chief sent his son to the scene. The next morning, Prosecutor Yang went to the Nanyi Yizhong Cemetery to open the coffin for autopsy as prescribed by law. Jiang Cairong and others avoided coming to the scene. The autopsy revealed that the corpse had been injured on the left cheek before falling into the water and drowning. He ordered the corpse to be reburied. After returning to the court, Prosecutor Yang ordered the relevant parties to be interrogated.

Jiaxing 101

Deadline for Solving the Dayun Temple Case

Dayun Temple Town, located at the intersection of Jiaxing and Jiashan, was robbed by bandits on the afternoon of February 16. More than ten men and women were kidnapped. The authorities of the two counties considered the case to be serious and sent water and land police to rescue the kidnapped people and pursue the stolen goods. However, many days passed without catching a single thief. Some of the more than ten kidnapped people have been released by the bandits. Cao Yueshan, Cao Diguan, Shen Shunqiu, Yao Lanqing, Bao Hushi, Liu Zhanggao and other six people are still in danger and their whereabouts are unknown, making it impossible to rescue them. It is reported that the provincial government is paying close attention to this case and has set a deadline of ten days for the Water Police District Chief of the Second District to solve the case. District Chief Zhao believes that since Jiangsu and Zhejiang have announced joint defense, bandits can be pursued regardless of provincial boundaries. Therefore, he has personally taken his troops to patrol the areas where Jiangsu and Zhejiang intersect.

Yangzhou 102

Order to Stop Collecting Rent

The county government previously received an order from Provincial Treasurer Guo to collect urban and rural rent for January and February of the 21st year to be handed over to the provincial treasury to meet urgent needs. The former County Magistrate Yang ordered the Public Security Bureau to investigate and collect the rent accordingly. Later, the bureau reported that it had collected 39,275.90 yuan as of November of that year. The county government stated that it was difficult to collect the remaining amount and requested that it be exempted. Now, the provincial government has ordered that the collection of uncollected rent be stopped as of the date of the order and that this be announced.

Zhenjiang 103

Zhenjiang Library Opens

The Zhenjiang Provincial Library in Taiping Bridge has been in preparation for nearly a year. The library will open its newspaper reading room, magazine reading room, and book reading room yesterday. The newspaper room has dozens of newspapers from the provincial capital, Beijing, Pingjin, Shanghai, Hankou, and English and Japanese newspapers. The magazine room has four or five hundred foreign and domestic periodicals of various subjects, all arranged on shelves for people to read. The reference book shelves in the book room also have dozens of dictionaries and yearbooks on various subjects. There are instructors in the room to provide guidance on how to search and use reference books, which is very thoughtful. The library currently has 40,000 books, and many more ordered from abroad have not yet arrived. Yesterday was the first day of opening, and according to statistics in the afternoon, there were more than 300 people reading newspapers and magazines and about dozens of people reading books in the book room. Most of the books read were in literature and social sciences. The library is open as usual on Sunday mornings. It is closed on Monday for holidays. To facilitate public officials, it is also open for two hours every night from Tuesday to Saturday.

Zhejiang Finance Department Allocates

Tuition Fees for Police Cadets Studying in Austria

The Zhejiang Provincial Government has repeatedly received telegrams from Minister of Education Zhu Jiahua, stating that the tuition fees for Zhejiang police cadets studying in Austria have been in arrears for half a year, causing them financial difficulties. Yesterday, it remitted another 4,500 yuan for the expenses for January, February, and March of this year to Vienna for the students to receive.

Yixing 105

Bandit Han Guilin Arrested

Che Qifeng's mother, from Chejiatang, Shili Village, on the northern outskirts of this county, was kidnapped by bandits on the night of May 30 of the year before last. A large sum of money was extorted, and three days later, she was brutally murdered and her body was abandoned in the western suburbs. The county government conducted an autopsy. In July of that year, Water Police Inspector Sun Meizhang arrested a bandit named Wang Wenbiao and sent him to the county for legal action. On September 7 of that year, the stationed troops successively arrested Wang Chuanren and Wang Ruming. Wang Wenbiao was summoned for questioning, and all confessed to the details of the case. The Pacification Superintendent's Office and the Provincial Security Office sentenced them to death. However, the bandit Han Zhulin had heard of the incident and fled far away. He returned to the urban area last winter and colluded with local ruffians to plot wrongdoing. After someone informed on him, he could not escape. The county government sent Detective Pan Jie to Wangjiayuan, in the back of the county, on the morning of the 4th to arrest Han Guilin. He was taken back and reported to the team. He was severely interrogated and handed over to the county for strict handling according to the law.

Huzhou 106

Bandits Rob, Kidnap Father and Kill Son

Wang Dongyang, a farmer from Xichajiadou, about seven miles from Yuanjiahuijie in the southern part of Huzhou, was targeted by bandits because of his modest wealth. On the night of the 3rd of this month, more than ten bandits suddenly came, carrying electric torches and wooden guns. They broke down the door and entered, turning over boxes and cabinets and looting at will. They stole all the gold, silver jewelry, and more than 40 carts of silkworm silk, causing a loss of more than 2,000 yuan. Before leaving, they kidnapped Wang Dongyang and took him down to the boat, and shot and killed Dongyang's son Yuanqing. Afterwards, Wang Dongyang's grandson, Meisheng, reported the incident to the military and police agencies in the city, requesting them to pursue the bandits.

Theft on Small Steamers on the Suzhou-Hangzhou-Huzhou Route 107

The small steamers of the Tongyuan Shipping Bureau on the Suzhou-Hangzhou-Huzhou route were sailing from Hangzhou to Huzhou on the evening of the 3rd when more than 20 bandits suddenly ordered the ships to stop near Gancun, near Linghu. They boarded the ships with weapons and looted the ships, stealing all the clothes and silver dollars from the passengers on the incense boats being towed by the steamers, causing a loss of more than 1,000 yuan.

Local News

The Financial Crisis in the United States Will Not Greatly Affect This City 108

The Gold Exchange Held an Important Meeting Yesterday

The financial crisis in the United States is expanding, and there is also talk of abolishing the gold standard. As a result, financial markets in various countries will undergo drastic changes. Yesterday, the gold market in this city was also affected, causing the standard gold price to plummet, causing extreme panic. The details are as follows:

Financial Community's Statement 109

A reporter from the New Voice News Agency specifically interviewed a certain member of the banking community in this city to inquire about how the Chinese banking community is dealing with the current financial disaster in the United States. The reply was, "The domestic recession in the United States has reached its extreme in recent years, so even though it is known as the 'Yellow Gold' country, it is still inevitable. The occurrence of this crisis has significantly affected countries in Europe and the United States. In the Far East, Japan has closer financial ties with the United States, and has suspended foreign exchange starting today. The exchange has also announced a temporary suspension. The severity of the situation is truly rare. As for our country, because the financial relationship with the United States is relatively shallow, in terms of debt, we only owe money to the United States. Therefore, this disaster will not have much of an impact."

Two Emergency Meetings 110

The New Voice News Agency reports that the Bankers Association held an emergency meeting at 2:00 PM yesterday. It is understood that the meeting was to discuss the response and maintenance measures for the plummeting standard gold price and the issue of the United States abolishing the gold standard. However, the results have not yet been announced. The board of directors of the Gold Exchange also met at 3:00 PM to discuss this issue. It was initially rumored that the market would be temporarily suspended due to the excessive decline. However, although the discussion had not yet concluded by 4:30 PM, there was no accurate news of a market shutdown. Therefore, the market will still open as usual today. As for the content of the meeting, it is difficult to ascertain due to strict confidentiality.

Shanghai American Businesses Operate as Usual 111

The "Ta Mei Evening News" reports that although American banks have suspended operations, the four American banks in this city are operating as usual today (the 6th). Furthermore, American Express and Thomas Cook are also operating as usual. However, there are some difficulties concerning the exchange of U.S. dollars due to the lack of exchange rates. Traveler's checks and money orders are being cashed as usual. The only difference today from usual is the difficulty in determining the price of U.S. dollars. Therefore, some banks have set temporary prices, while others pay in silver first and then settle the difference later. For example, Citibank and Chase Bank are handling U.S. dollar accounts and customers in this way. American Foreign Insurance Association and American Oriental Bank, which operate Far Eastern trade, both have their headquarters in Shanghai and are not affected by the suspension of American banks, are now also adopting the same procedures. Some shipping companies are crediting U.S. dollars first and settling later, while others are calculating according to temporary exchange rates. The prices offered by various Chinese small money shops vary from four yuan and eight jiao to four yuan and six jiao, while the purchase prices vary from four yuan and one jiao to four yuan and two jiao. It is said that there has been little trading.

Rice Industry Unrest Expands 112

Shipping Merchants Block Rice Boats from Coming to Shanghai

Guild Requests City Government to Stop It

Gu Xin'yi, Chairman of the Bean and Rice Guild, and Lu Wenshao, Chairman of the Rice Shop Guild, went to the Municipal Government yesterday afternoon to ask the Mayor to stop the shipping merchants from obstructing transportation. Regarding the issue of heavy measures (of rice), the Party and government organs consulted yesterday and decided to formulate a compromise solution and schedule a public discussion with rice industry groups. The details are as follows:

Rice Industry Demands Halt to Obstruction of Transportation 113

Yesterday afternoon at 4 p.m., Gu Xin'yi, Chairman of the Bean and Rice Guild, and Lu Wenshao, Chairman of the Rice Shop Guild, went to the Municipal Government at Fenglin Bridge to request that the obstruction of transportation be stopped. As Mayor Wu was engaged in official business, he specially appointed Hong Da, Section Chief of the Second Section, to receive them. The two representatives, Gu and Lu, explained that the shipping merchants were obstructing rice boats from coming to Shanghai and that they had gathered crowds to beat and injure many boatmen and to cause trouble for various businesses. They requested the Municipal Government to order the Water Patrol Team to cooperate with the Public Security Bureau to stop the shipping merchants from obstructing transportation. Section Chief Hong promised to report this to Mayor Wu and then handle it.

Guild Advocates Abolishing Volume Measures and Adopting Weight Measures 114

The Shanghai Bean and Rice Trade Guild submitted a report to the Shanghai Municipal Government yesterday, stating: "Regarding the rice merchants from southern Shanghai who are obstructing transportation under the pretext of heavy measures and using this as a means of coercion, we respectfully request strict orders to arrest and apprehend them and, at the same time, to permit the abolition of volume measures and the adoption of weight measures in order to quell disputes and eliminate hidden dangers. It is humbly submitted that measuring instruments have been used in society for a long time. Guild members have been trading in and out of rice measures (shi) with the custom of being filled to the brim, and there has never been a dispute over heavy measures. Boatmen from Wuxi, Changshu, Songjiang, Qingpu, Jiaoli, Pinghu, Xincang, Jiaxing, Xindi, Zhujing, Sijing, Fengjing, Suzhou, Beizha, Lili, Zhouzhuang, Tongli and other ports have been transporting back and forth like shuttles, and merchants have been getting along without any differences. Recently, however, a so-called Alliance Association of Rice Merchants from Southern Shanghai has been nitpicking at the measurers on the pretext of heavy measures. When their intentions are not fulfilled, they obstruct transportation as a means of coercion. The old tricks that they used last September and October are being re-enacted today."

Chicago Expo Preparatory Committee to Return Exhibits Starting Today 115

U.S. Counselor Cables that U.S. Retains Chinese Pavilion

He Bingxian and Others Resign from Association Positions

After the preparations for China's participation in the Chicago Exposition were completed, it was decided that the solicited exhibits would be returned starting today. The Products Association is scheduled to host a banquet for the U.S. Commercial Counselor tonight, and He Bingxian and others have submitted letters of resignation from their positions as directors of the Association. The details are as follows:

Announcement Regarding the Return of Exhibits 116

After the Exhibition of Solicited Exhibits closed the night before last, the Preparatory Committee decided to begin returning the solicited exhibits from various provinces and cities starting today. Once the exhibit certificates are printed, they will be issued. The announcement from the Exhibit Department is as follows: "The Exhibition of Solicited Exhibits held by this Association in Shanghai closed on March 5th. Since the Chicago Expo has been canceled, we are proceeding with the winding-up process. In addition to sending separate letters, all exhibitors in Shanghai are requested to send representatives to the office of this Association at the National Central Research Institute, No. 947 Bailinan Road, between 9:00 a.m. and 12:00 p.m. and between 2:00 p.m. and 5:00 p.m. daily from March 7th to March 11th, bringing the original receipts, to collect their exhibits in accordance with their original application forms. Please do not delay. This is hereby announced."

U.S. Counselor Cables U.S. Yesterday 117

In addition to telegraphing the Chicago Exposition to retain the Chinese Pavilion, the Products Association sent Zhou Guanhong to visit Andrew Roth, the U.S. Commercial Counselor in China, at 10:00 a.m. yesterday to request its retention and explain the reasons. It was decided that a banquet would be held for Andrew Roth at the Taolechun Sichuan Restaurant on Sanma Road at 7:30 p.m. today. Andrew Roth cabled the U.S. city of Mei (transliteration) last night, stating: "Mr. Alberdi from Washington to Chicago, the China Products Association wishes to retain the name of the Chinese group and voluntarily participate in the Chicago Expo. The previously authorized Chinese venue area, measuring 20,000 square feet, is still hoped to be granted to the Products Association. The venue construction costs can be undertaken for 50,000 yuan. With the exhibition period approaching, a reply is urgently requested."

Letters of Resignation from He Bingxian and Others 118

After the Products Association nominated fifteen directors, He Bingxian, Cai Wuji, Zhang Xianglin, Miao Zhongxiu, and others sent letters to the Products Association yesterday, resigning from their positions as directors. They wrote: "Regarding participation in the Chicago Exposition, after reading today's newspaper, we learned that your Association has nominated Bingxian and others as officers, and we dare not disobey. However, Bingxian and others were originally members of the Preparatory Committee and were appointed by the government order. We are now under orders to expedite the winding-up process and are unable to participate in the Association. We earnestly request that other capable individuals be nominated to avoid delaying the process. If there is anything we can do to help, we will wholeheartedly support it in our individual capacities to live up to your earnest friendship. We hereby respectfully decline and hope for your understanding. We would be grateful beyond measure."

Municipal Chamber of Commerce Cables Zhang Xueliang 120

Urgently Devise Plans to Redeem Himself

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce telegraphed Zhang Xueliang yesterday, stating: "To Zhang, Acting Chairman of the Beiping Military Branch: The disaster in Rehe, in less than ten days, has completely fallen into enemy hands. Since you separately appointed a commander, it was early knowledge that Tang was difficult to bear the sole command. Shanghai Post Office Stops Sending Packages to Rehe 122

The General Bureau Has Not Received a Report from the Tianjin Bureau

The Suspension of Sending is of a Temporary Nature

After news of the fall of Chengde reached Shanghai, the Parcel Office of the Shanghai Postal Administration suspended the acceptance of parcels destined for all parts of Rehe starting yesterday morning. Letters are still being accepted, but there are very few. As of yesterday afternoon, the General Bureau had not yet received a report from the Tianjin Post Office regarding postal services in Rehe Province. Therefore, the General Bureau has not issued a circular regarding the suspension of mail to Rehe. The suspension of sending those parcels is only a temporary measure. In the future, regarding mail to Rehe, what should be suspended and what should be accepted will be determined after the report from the Tianjin Bureau arrives in Shanghai. Furthermore, according to Kang Yong, a standing committee member of the Postal Workers' Union, regarding the safety of postal workers in various parts of Rehe, the union has telegraphed the Beiping Workers' Union to find ways to evacuate them in batches, and there should be no danger.

Zhu Jiqing's Circular Telegram 123

"Today, there is either the enemy or me; either me or the enemy.

To seek national survival, only iron and blood will do."

The Shanghai Liaison Office of the Northeast National Salvation Army Command Headquarters received a rush telegram from Zhu Jiqing yesterday, stating: "To be distributed to all newspapers for the information of all compatriots: From the day this army was organized, it has been determined to fight the violent Japanese to the death. Even though we are surrounded by a strong enemy and bombarded by artillery fire, we dare not be timid or retreat. As long as there is a breath of life, this determination will not waver. Now, the enemy's atmosphere is intensifying day by day, and Rehe cannot be defended. This is the autumn of our nation's crisis and survival, and it is also the day when our people struggle for the nation. In the past, when the country was not well-established and internal strife was frequent, it could still be attributed to personal struggles for power, which had nothing to do with the common people. Now, however, the survival of the nation is at stake. To be masters or slaves is a matter of utmost urgency. Our ancestors braved thorns and established a great land for us descendants to live and thrive on. How can we sit idly by and allow it to be slaughtered by foreign races? In the past, during the September 18th Incident, we lost the three eastern provinces due to non-resistance. Now, although we are barely resisting, we are passive everywhere. The enemy gains the upper hand and we have no time to defend ourselves. We collapse without fighting. Moreover, there are still some generals who usually consider it their ability to withhold salaries and disturb the people, and at the critical moment, they panic and lose their composure. The enemy has not arrived, but they flee first, causing the entire army to be affected. Our people should request the government to inspire the hearts of the soldiers, strictly enforce military law, turn defense into offense, and fight to the death with the enemy. We must know that in today's situation, there is either the enemy or me; either me or the enemy. To seek the survival of the nation, only iron and blood will do. We hope that our people will all tremble at the crisis of the nation and rise up to urgently plan for it. Zhu Jiqing, rush."

Date of Wang Jingwei's Return to China 124

French Postal Company Cables That He Will Arrive in Shanghai on the 17th

The French Postal Shipping Company received a cable from its headquarters in France yesterday, stating that Wang Jingwei, the President of the Executive Yuan of China, has taken the company's postal ship Aramis back to China and is expected to arrive in port around the 17th of this month.

Now, obstruction of transportation is not enough, so it is followed by blocking navigation. Blocking navigation is not enough, so it is increased by acts of violence. Minhang and Huangdu have both been blocked. However, this city is not a rice-producing area, and the food for the citizens depends on supplies from the interior. Now that the Alliance Association has obstructed transportation for more than half a month, fortunately, there are stocks of goods from Hunan, Anhui, and Jiangxi provinces to trade with, so no panic has occurred. If the problem is not resolved for a long time and at the same time rice merchants also disregard the overall situation and adopt a go-slow approach, then the danger of a shortage is imminent. At this time when the national crisis is pressing, the order in the rear is suddenly disrupted, and who will be blamed? I believe that the way to solve the problem is to deal with it fairly. The focus of the Alliance Association's dispute is the accusation of heavy measures. Then, it is possible to abandon volume measures and adopt weight measures. In the past, imported rice and domestic Hunan, Anhui, and Jiangxi rice have all been packaged and weighed for sale, and there has been no objection since trading. Some people may think that volume measures are used in the interior, and weight measures are used in Shanghai. It is inconvenient to use volume measures for entry and weight measures for exit. However, if the rice merchants in the interior all have the concept of heavy measures as claimed by the Alliance Association, then they will certainly be happy to express their sympathy for the abolition of volume measures and the adoption of weight measures. From now on, packaging and weighing should be used for all transactions, and there is no need to seek convenience. Some people may think that the counting of weights may not be accurate. However, valuable items such as silkworm cocoons are bought and sold entirely by weight, and we have never heard of them being abandoned due to inaccuracy. And the purchase and sale of rice measures worth eight or nine yuan is the only concern because it is feared that they are not accurate, which is also unreasonable. Some people may think that rice has moisture and that transportation takes time. If weight measures are used, the loss is difficult to predict. The moisture of rice is a matter of quality. The quality is good or bad, and there is a market price to distinguish it. Weight measures are used to calculate the quantity of rice, and what does it have to do with moisture? Moreover, the time it takes for imported rice and Hunan, Anhui, and Jiangxi rice to be transported to Shanghai is the same as in the interior. However, we have never heard of anyone complaining about the weight measures due to the moisture of rice. The above-mentioned rice purchases and sales should be changed to weight measures, which is fair for entry and exit and leaves no room for doubt. Therefore, since the Alliance Association accused the use of heavy measures and obstructed transportation, the association believes that the most straightforward and fair way to resolve this dispute is to abolish volume measures and adopt weight measures. If we abandon this and use a funnel, the Shanghai Bureau of Weights and Measures has conducted a trial, and according to the results of the trial, it is considered to be inconvenient in many ways. It takes 18 seconds to measure each measure with a funnel, while it only takes 3 seconds with a basket. It is estimated that the daily rice trade in this city is about 13,000 measures, and it is not allowed by time to measure rice with a funnel. This is an indisputable fact in the report of Director Zhou. Now the Alliance Association is still crying as if it is impossible not to use a funnel, and it is really unclear what they intend. Now, the Alliance Association has obstructed transportation for more than half a month. If we do not take urgent action, the food supply for the citizens of this city will be in danger of panic. Therefore, we are urgently and fully appealing for your review, and quickly send official letters to the Shanghai County Government where Minhang is located and the Jiading County Government where Huangdu is located. On the one hand, strictly order the Municipal Public Security Bureau to send police to go to the respective county police officers to strictly arrest and punish the lawless thugs who are obstructing rice navigation. On the other hand, allow the abolition of volume measures and the adoption of weight measures, and order the Alliance Association to resume navigation as soon as possible to maintain law and order and to protect people's food. We cannot but await your orders in trepidation. Respectfully submitted to Mayor Wu of the Shanghai Municipal Government."

Party and Government Change the Method of Disposal 125

The Dagong Agency reports that the Municipal Party Headquarters and the Social Affairs Bureau conducted a final decision on the selection of leveled measures, funnels, and the adoption of weight measures at 2 p.m. yesterday. However, because the rice industry groups are complex and opinions are divided, the original plan has been completely changed. It is planned to formulate another compromise solution and convene rice industry groups again on the 9th of this month for public discussion.

Kong Xiangxi Arrived in Shanghai Last Night 128

Delegation Secretary Zheng Yanfen Came Along

Kong Talked About His Deep Impressions of His Travels in Europe

Countries Are Too Busy to Take Care of Themselves and Cannot Afford to Help Others

Hoping That the People Will Wake Up, Rise Up, and Save Themselves

Kong Xiangxi, the special envoy sent by the National Government to Europe and the United States to investigate industries, went abroad in mid-September last year and traveled to various countries in Europe and the United States for half a year. Yesterday, at 7:30 p.m., he took the Italian postal ship Conte Verde to return to Shanghai. After Kong landed, he went straight to his private residence to rest and meet with reporters from various newspapers to talk about his impressions of his travels in Europe and the United States. The details are as follows:

Welcome at the Port 129

Around 6 p.m. yesterday evening, those who went to the Hongkou Gonghexiang Pier to welcome him included Mayor Wu Tiecheng, Secretary-General of the Executive Yuan Chu Minyi, Mrs. Sun Yat-sen Soong Ching-ling, former Vice Minister of Industry Zheng Hongnian, Zhao Jinqing, Jianghai Customs Superintendent Tang Hai'an, Secretary Tang Zhaoshi, former Foreign Minister Wang Zhengting, Director of the Municipal Public Security Bureau Wen Hongen, Secretary Zhao Tiezhang of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs Office in Shanghai, Dean Song's wife, Ms. Zhang Le Yi, as well as Kong's wife Soong Ai-ling, and Soong Zi-liang, Soong Zi-an, National League of Nations Transportation Commissioner Qi Ya Long, as well as former colleagues of the Ministry of Industry, totaling more than 100 people.

Arrival in Shanghai 130

The Italian ship Conte Verde, on which Kong was traveling, entered Wusongkou at 5:30 p.m. yesterday and docked at the Gonghexiang Pier on East Broadway at 7 p.m. After the gangway was set up, Mrs. Kong, accompanied by Soong Ching-ling and Soong Zi-liang, was the first to board the ship. Then, the welcomers also followed each other up. Kong's secretaries Xu Jianping and Customs Superintendent Tang Hai'an received them. The welcomers entered the first-class cabin hall to meet with Kong. Kong shook hands with Sun Yat-sen's wife, Wang Zhengting, Wu Tiecheng, Chu Minyi, and other dignitaries, as well as other welcomers, and exchanged pleasantries. He then disembarked at 7:40 p.m. and took a car with Mrs. Kong back to his residence on West Ams Road in the French Concession to rest.

Report to Chiang 131

Those who came with Kong were still the three secretaries who went with him: Zhu Maocheng, Xu Jianping, and Li Tang. In addition, Zheng Yanfang, the secretary of the Chinese delegation sent by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to attend the League of Nations conference in Geneva, also came on the same ship as Kong. After landing, Zheng took a car to the hotel to rest. After Kong and others arrived at the residence, Song Ziwen, the Acting President of the Executive Yuan, had already arrived. They talked for a while and telegraphed Chairman Chiang to report that he had returned to Shanghai safely.

Impressions of Traveling Abroad 132

Kong then met with reporters from various newspapers at his residence and first described his impressions of his trip to Europe and the United States. The deepest impression I got from this trip to Europe and the United States was that although all countries are in extremely difficult situations, they are still able to work together to find solutions. Take the United Kingdom as an example. The war debt issue, the unemployment issue, and the Irish issue are pressing down layer upon layer. However, the United Kingdom is still able to overcome all difficulties and deal with them in an unusually thorough manner. Take Germany as an example. After the European War, Germany was almost bankrupt. Unemployment was everywhere. Not only did university graduates have no way out, but even those with specialized skills could not find a place to make a living. Although Germany was in this desperate situation, it still made every effort to cope. The reason why Hitler was able to gain the belief of a small number of people in this election was that the German people hoped that Hitler could concentrate power in the central government to save Germany from its predicament. Take Italy as an example. Italy was divided and chaotic in the past few decades. Even the trains were often delayed for four or five hours. However, since Mussolini came to power, Italy has become a new emerging power. The Italian ship that I took today takes only 25 days from Europe to the East, and its speed is unmatched by other countries' ships. In short, there have been many changes in European countries after the war, but they are all urgently seeking self-rescue and have no time to pay attention to the East. Although the League of Nations has passed reports, it is unlikely to make further substantive sanctions. The same is true for the United States. It is indeed well-disposed towards us, but it cannot shed blood and fight for us. In short, now that the national crisis has reached this point, we can only work together to save ourselves. As for the results of my investigation into the industries and economy of Europe and the United States, I will disclose them all at a later date."

Defending Against Insults with Strength 133

Kong continued, "While I was on the ship, I heard the news of the fall of Chifeng and Chengde and felt even more indignant. When I was in Europe, there were many people in various countries who upheld justice and expressed sympathy, but because of various difficult problems, they could not give us substantive assistance. Heaven helps those who help themselves. The Chinese people should be aware of this. People from all countries are also asking why China does not unite against foreign countries in the midst of national disasters, but instead hopes that other countries will take up their grievances. It is known that relying on others is unreliable, and Japan is even carrying out various insults and national propaganda in Europe and the United States to confuse international public opinion. How should our country unite from top to bottom and defend against insults with strength to show our country's determination to resist the violence of others? Otherwise, we can only sit and listen to being slaughtered."

To Nanjing Via Japan 134

Kong said at the end, "When I passed through Hong Kong this time, I made an appointment with Mr. Hu Zhantang, but because of the urgency of time, I was unable to meet with him. I plan to go to Nanjing via Japan in the next few days to report everything to the Central Government." After Kong finished speaking, someone asked if he would be going to the post of Minister to Italy. Kong resolutely replied, "Now is not the time to be a Minister. We must rush to the border and join the front line to fight the enemy to the death!"

"We Chinese citizens are our own. Today, I am grateful to all of you who are present, although you are my personal friends, but you all have great prestige in the military, political, business, academic, and other circles in this city. I know that you are very enthusiastic about the cause of saving the country. So today, I sincerely invite you to be members of our team. The letters of invitation will be sent separately. I also hope that you will give us more guidance today, either on the recruitment of members of the Aviation Association, or on the current serious situation. I would like to raise a glass of clear wine to wish you good health and to work hard to carry out the 'aviation to save the country' movement and complete the great cause of 'aviation to save the country.'"

Freight Train and Locomotive Derailed on the Jinghu Railway 143

After 7:30 Yesterday Morning

Passing Through Qishuyan Station

Derailed Due to Incorrectly Switched Points

At 7:35 yesterday morning, the Jinghu Railway's northbound freight train No. 335 derailed at Qishuyan Station because the pointsman at the station mistakenly switched the points, causing the locomotive to derail and sink, crushing two steel rails and two sleepers. Traffic was completely blocked. The stationmaster immediately sent an urgent telegram for help. Subsequently, senior staff from the railway's Changzhou-based traffic, engineering, and machinery departments supervised workers, dispatched a rescue train, and went to repair the line. The main line was temporarily reconnected at 11:30 am to allow trains to pass, but trains could not cross, and the speed had to be reduced. The derailed locomotive was put back on the track at 1:45 pm, and then both the main and branch lines were repaired, and the work was completed at 6:10 pm. Therefore, yesterday's north- and southbound trains on the Jinghu Railway were delayed by several hours.

Song Ziwen Inspected Relocated Antiquities in Shanghai Yesterday 144

Tagged and Sealed by the Executive Yuan in the Afternoon

Iron Net Constructed All Around Under Strict Martial Law

The Guowen News Agency reports that 1,054 boxes of antiquities from the Palace Museum in Beiping were transported to Shanghai the day before yesterday and stored at the former site of Renji at 26 Tianzhutang Street. The entire storage process was not completed until 8 pm the night before. At that time, the authorities of the Chinese and French concessions dispatched police to guard and protect the site. All warehouse doors were sealed with seals from the Executive Yuan. Yesterday, the reporter returned to the site and saw Secretary Wu Ying and his staff affixing Executive Yuan seals to each box and assigning numbers. At 11 am, Song Ziwen, acting President of the Executive Yuan, and Li Zongdong, Secretary-General of the Museum, personally went to the warehouse to inspect the antiquities. Not long after, Liu Hongsheng, manager of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, also arrived to visit. Song left after staying for about 20 minutes. According to Secretary Wu Ying, the date for the shipment of the second batch of transported antiquities has not yet been set. Secretary-General Li Zongdong will not go to Beijing today. The antiquities are related to the national essence, so they were escorted from Peiping to Shanghai. In addition to a portion of the staff remaining in Beijing, eight staff members, including Yi Xianmo and Na Zhiliang, led by me (Wu referred to himself), have come here to manage the antiquities temporarily. No management office or similar name will be set up downstairs. Only one room will be opened as a dormitory for care. After the conversation, the reporter departed and saw that an iron net had been constructed around the warehouse. Wooden posts had also been erected along the open space on the side of Tianzhutang Street to build an iron net, but a pit was dug in the middle, presumably for guards to stay. A small house was built on the northeast corner of the platform on the sixth floor for observation. The entrance was guarded by Annamese police. There was a guard at every door inside, so the protection was very strict.

China Factory Inspection Association Discussed Factory Inspection in the Special Zone Yesterday 147

Opposing Foreign Interference with China's Authority

Statement to be Issued and Meeting Scheduled with Various Sectors

The China Factory Inspection Association held an interim meeting yesterday afternoon at the Eight Immortals Bridge Public Welfare Association. Thirty-odd members attended, including Shen Risheng and Wang Rangcheng. Tian Heqing was the chairman, and Li De was the recording secretary. First, the chairman reported the purpose of the meeting: (1) Major tragedies have occurred successively in the Zhengtai and Yonghe rubber factories in the city, and people from all walks of life feel the importance of factory safety. The association plans to prepare a periodical to disseminate safety knowledge; (2) The follow-up measures for disasters in factories are not entirely consistent with laws and regulations. Should the association make any statement? (3) The authorities in the Shanghai Special Zone have repeatedly obstructed the Chinese government from sending personnel to inspect factories in the Special Zone, and there are many obstacles to the progress. This move by the authorities in the Special Zone has no legal basis, but it has a huge impact on both factories and workers. The association is more aware of the situation and should explain it to all parties. After the report, the discussion began. (1) Regarding the association's periodical, it was resolved to postpone publication due to economic reasons; (2) Regarding the follow-up measures for the disasters in the Zhengtai and Yonghe rubber factories, it was resolved that since there are clear provisions in the Factory Law, the association does not need to make a statement for the time being; (3) Regarding how the Shanghai Special Zone authorities should be made to stop obstructing the Chinese government from sending personnel to inspect factories, it was resolved that: A. The association should issue a statement explaining the process of the Special Zone authorities obstructing factory inspections and the reasons why it is inappropriate to seize factory inspection authority; B. The association should regularly invite the local press and invite industrial and commercial groups to discuss everything; (4) Regarding establishing a Chinese factory inspection system, it was resolved that a request should be submitted to the central government to quickly establish a Chinese factory inspection system so that it can be implemented in various places as soon as possible.
