Business Classics (16) 253

Advantages of Domestically Produced White Sugar 254

Is Beneficial to Agriculture and Widely Accessible. Occupying an Important Position in Food. Since the Flourishing of Foreign Goods, Domestically Produced Goods Have Faced Difficulties. The Situation Continues Uninterrupted. The Situation of Foreign Goods Usurping the Position of the Host. Still, Domestically Produced Goods Are Superior to Foreign Goods. Now is the Time When Foreign Goods Are Flooding the Market. [We] Will Introduce in Installments to the People Various Types of Goods, Their Names, and Characteristics. Report With Plans to Revitalize and Safeguard Our Rights. This Article Will Focus on White Sugar.

"Tribute Powder" is produced in Zhangzhou, Fujian. It is made from the top layer of sugar juice, so it is exceptionally sweet and has a pure, shiny color. The quality is dry and pure, and it dissolves without residue. It is the highest-grade domestically produced white sugar. We have not seen this grade of goods for over a dozen years. It is said that sugar production will increase in the future and may reappear. "Packaging Method": Packaged in baskets, covered with cloth bags and tied, or in double burlap bags.

"Quanzhou White" is produced in Quanzhou, Fujian. The color is slightly inferior to "Tribute Powder," and the quality and aroma are also lower. However, the sweetness is similar. (Packaging Method) Double burlap wrapped and tied.

"Xinghua White" is produced in Xinghua Prefecture, Fujian. The color is like Quanzhou White, but the quality is coarser and the sweetness is adequate. (Method of Use) Same as above.

"Zuojiang White" is produced in Zuojiang, Guangxi. The color is as white as TaiKoo's Three-Temperature-and-a-Half Sugar, the texture is fine and clean, and it also has aroma and adequate sweetness. (Packaging Method) Same as above.

"Yangli White" is produced in Yangli, Guangxi. What is now called Nali White is this type. The color is similar to Zuojiang White, with slight variations. The sweetness is adequate, but the aroma is less. (Packaging Method) Same as above.

"Qinzhou Second White" is produced in Qinzhou. It is like light wine, slightly fermented. It is soft in texture and adequately sweet. (Packaging Method) Same as above.

"Hui'an Second White" is produced in Hui'an. The color is slightly lighter than Qinzhou goods. It has no aroma, is drier, and is adequately sweet. (Packaging Method) Same as above.

"Mianhu White" is produced in Chaozhou. It is white in color and excessively sweet. It is divided into five types, with the highest grade being "Zu San Jian" (足三肩). The color is as white as TaiKoo's Four-Temperature Sugar, and the sweetness surpasses it. The texture is neither dry nor wet and is fine. (Function) If you would use 10 catties of foreign sugar, this grade requires only 8 catties. The next grade is "Zu Bing" (足冰). The color is as white as TaiKoo's Three-Temperature-and-a-Half Sugar, and the other characteristics are the same as above. The next grade is "Binghua White" (冰花白). The color is as white as TaiKoo's Three-Two-Five Sugar, and the other characteristics are the same as above. The next grade is "Shuang Gai" (雙蓋). The color is like TaiKoo's Three-Temperature Sugar, the texture is slightly coarser, and the other characteristics are the same as above. The lowest grade is "Dan Gai" (單蓋). The color is like light-colored brown sugar, and the texture and sweetness are the same as above. (Packaging Method) Inner bamboo basket, outer cloth wrap, tied with rope.

"Huizhou White" is produced in Huizhou. The color is white, similar to upper Bing, but the aroma is slightly inferior, the texture is fine, and the sweetness is adequate. (Packaging Method) Double cloth wrap, tied with double rattan.

"Qiongzhou White" is produced in Qiongzhou. The color, taste, texture, and packaging method are all the same as above.

"Huizhou Foreign" is produced in Huizhou. The color is as white as TaiKoo's Three-Temperature Sugar, the sweetness is adequate, and the texture is soft and glutinous. (Packaging Method) Same as above. In Summary, The Sweetness and Aroma of These Various Types of Domestically Produced White Sugar All Far Surpass Imported Goods. It's a Pity that Production is Limited, and Some Have Not Been Available for a Long Time. Now That Foreign Sugar is Becoming Expensive, Domestically Produced Sugar Has Room to Move, so Efforts Should Be Made to Promote It.

Essays

South Seas Native Antique Jar Gathering 255

— Zhan Lu

| No. 4 of World Customs and Ballads |

The natives have long resided in the South Seas islands, and love to collect antique jars as rare treasures. They are scattered like stars, never too many, and stacked like beds and houses, still feeling it's too few. Ask them how much property they have? Just count the jars to answer. The value of one jar can be a thousand gold pieces. One jar broken means a thousand gold pieces broken. Every spring and autumn, they host feasts for guests, and have a grand gathering of antique jars. They arrange rows of jars and urns, and among the layers, which is the most precious? Antique jars, antique jars, not all the same. Some are suitable for facing forward, some are suitable for facing sideways. The white ones have patterns like the belly of a fish, and the speckled ones can have colors like dragon scales. All kinds of colors are provided for guests to view, and red silk decorations are added everywhere. Praises rise, and the guests are happy. The host is delighted and has face. What is the pleasure of showing off? It is difficult for a king in the south to change this. If the guests are not satisfied, and think it is not enough to entertain their eyes, any sound of seeking flaws and finding fault is a great humiliation to the host. The distinction between honor and disgrace lies in a jar. Everyone loves to play with the jars and urns. Even if they go bankrupt, what does it matter? If the jar is good, its name crowns the crowd. Don't you see the South Seas village chief with his head held high? Ruling a village like a country. The people whisper in the streets, "This is the great king of antique jars." | Note: In wealthy South Seas families, no expense is spared to collect many fine jars. One need only be publicly recognized as the great king of antique jars, and that person has the hope of being elected as the leader of a village.

Eclecticism 256

— Yongzi

| Only I Am Supreme |

Once, I was sent on official business to a certain county in northern Jiangsu. Starting from the Shanghai office, I used a total of ten modes of transportation: tram, train, horse carriage, ferry boat, automobile, rickshaw, inland steamboat, wheelbarrow, roll ferry, and sampan. Finally, after disembarking from the sampan, I hired three round-headed, square-footed people who took turns carrying a small green-draped official sedan chair, entering the city with loud calls to clear the way. People avoided me, looking askance. I sat comfortably in the chair, looking down on everything, very majestic.

Considering that I, who have two crooked legs and brave wind, frost, rain, and snow, am squeezed in the distance between the office and the pavilion-style residence, and in the tens of thousands of people, I remember using eleven modes of transportation from different eras. Although this is not a brand new experience, I must carve out a piece of my heart to sing praises to all the scientists of the past and present, from ancient times to the present, from north to south, east to west, who have invented these many modes of transportation, neglecting sleep and food, and to all the great craftsmen who have labored hard to manufacture these many modes of transportation for us to enjoy. At the same time, I am even more grateful to my fellow Chinese compatriots who strive to preserve the national essence while also loving and adopting foreign goods. If China were not China, people in the 20th century would probably rarely be able to enjoy so many material civilizations in an orderly manner within three or four days, because many of these things have long been abandoned by people in Western civilized countries. This point, perhaps no one can laugh at. Because the great scientist who invented the airplane may not even match the variety of modes of transportation I sat on that time in his whole life, even though I have never taken the airplane that is supposed to save the country.

This eclectic situation, like ox urine and horse dung, or broken drum skin, perfectly symbolizes the Chinese national character. Classics must be zealously protected, slang is equally welcomed. Remaining loyal to one's husband is worthy of praise, while open marriage needs to be promoted urgently.

Wharf Pickup 257

— Yunshi

| On-Water Operations |

In every commercial port's inn for travelers, there is a special class of servant, different from the usual tea room staff, called "wharf pickup (接江)"; they don't rely on lighters (躉船), and travelers who are not used to it often think that this kind of operation has a bit of risk. As soon as they hear the steamship's whistle in the distance, they rush to their work as if flying. In ports like Shanghai, ships usually enter during the day, but in Zhenjiang, Nantong, Jiangyin, and other ports, ships often dock in the pitch-black night. Every time I go to Shanghai, before the ship docks, I see small sampans like floating gulls swarming to kiss the steamship, a group of so-called "wharf pickup" personnel. As soon as they touch an iron railing of the ship, or any place on the outer hull where they can put their feet, they climb up, as nimble as monkeys. In an instant, their shouts rise together, "Want to go to XXX?" "Want to go to XX?" shaking the entire ship. It is said that they are responsible for taking passengers back to the hotel, but they don't care about the trivial operations. Like the wharf pickup personnel operating along the Shanghai-Yangzhou line, their operations are even more laborious. If it is a traveler disembarking at Longwoko, they board the ship at Tianxingqiao on the river to pick up passengers. They also serve as both wharf pickup and drop-off personnel because these ports do not have lighters (躉船); passengers get on and off relying entirely on a number of sampans. If you are carrying a little luggage and don't have wharf pickup or drop-off personnel, you can't get on and off. Getting off the ship at these ports is often late at night. They brave wind and cold, eat in the rain and snow, cautiously take care of the passengers' luggage, and help them off the ship. When we accidentally pass by once, we always cry out in bitterness! They do this every day, making a living in this vast river. I once saw a wharf pickup personnel jump up when he was still five feet away from the ship, and the passengers all criticized him for taking such a risk. He calmly replied, "I'm used to it to get ahead of the others and pick up passengers." I couldn't help but sigh! "Nothing in the world is as difficult as earning a living!"

That year, the Datong Shipping Company's "New Daming" was deliberately rammed by the Japanese merchant ship "Atsuta" Maru for straying off the shipping route, and it is said that seven or eight wharf pickup personnel were killed. They could have avoided accidental dangers, not boarding the ship and walking dozens of miles to pick up passengers, but for business competition, they still scrambled to solve the bread problem on the water.

Border Ballad 258

— Zhen

Commander Su Gong Tie'an, a famous anti-Japanese general, was a refined and elegant Confucian general with peerless achievements in both poetry and literature. His poem "On Recalling the Past at Forty" has been echoed by many at home and abroad, and it has been praised as a masterpiece in literary circles. He and General Ma Zhanshan once fought against the violent Japanese with an isolated army in a remote area, and when the ammunition and supplies ran out, they retreated into Soviet Russia, and then his singing fell silent for a long time. Last year, he sent a letter to Cai Gong in Lingnan, containing four poems expressing his feelings at the end of the year, which were passionate and high-spirited, echoing through the heavens. His ambitions have not been fulfilled, alas, alas. I now record them below, when he was still stationed in Hailar. The beacon fires fill the sky and have not yet stopped. How many are drunk and how many are awake? I will use my iron blood to save the world, and occasionally write about my pure heart to nourish my soul. The snow covers the lonely city, and the reed pipes are blown hoarsely. The stars entwine the desert, and the sword light is bloody. (Liaoning, Jilin, and Heilongjiang have fallen one after another, and it is fortunate to be able to survive outside the Xing'an Mountains. Leaning on my sword and singing, I cannot help but feel melancholy.) Looking back on the events of the past twenty-five years, I have lost my youth and my temples are gray. (He left home and joined the army twenty-five years ago.) The banners shine brightly on the camp of ten thousand men. The old horses neigh sadly all night long. I still hope to repay my long-cherished wish to resist the enemy, and I cannot bear to let down the common people in securing the border. The war clouds pass by in the blink of an eye, leaving thousands of miles empty. The game of chess is sad, and another game is lost. Reining in my horse and looking from a high point in the western mountains, where is the Great Wall? The crane's warning consumes effort in strategic planning. I compete to see the pillar standing firm in the middle of the current. The sword energy flies up to the heavens, and the military sound is awakened, shaking the Dipper constellation. Righteousness has the song of Wen Songrui, and devotion to the country has the Marquis of Wu. (He admired Marquis Wu and Wen Songrui the most in his life.) Studying green history by the light of a lamp at the end of the night, who can compare with the ancients in all ages? Snowflakes like palms press on the saddle, and the watchman's clapper is desolate, and another year ends. For two years, we have been gnashing our teeth in the same hatred. (In the defense against Russia, Generals Han and Wei were killed in action. On the second anniversary, he specially sent Chief of Staff Wang to cross the border to the tombs of the two generals to represent him in paying respects, recalling their loyalty and mourning their deaths.) I entrust the three borders again alone with my liver and guts. Clouds lie across the ancient fortress, and the lonely smoke is straight. The wind rolls the clear sand, and the setting sun is cold. I carry the heavy burden of home and country on one shoulder, and I do not have time to rest morning and night. (Moved to help the Northeast Volunteer Army.)

Full-Length Novel

The Fourth Company Commander of the Northeast 260

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter 1: Pushing Food With Attentive Solicitude, He Specifically Invites a Poor Girl to Recall; People Are Generous and Uniquely Possess the Heroism of a Warrior

When it was almost dark, the servant of the Gan family stood outside the courtyard and shouted, "Old Lady, is your millet porridge ready yet? Our Second Master told us to get some porridge." Madam Jiang was puzzled, "How would he know we're cooking porridge?" She replied, "It's ready. Come and get some." The elder daughter quickly took the porcelain pot into the house, filled it full of porridge, and held it out with both hands. Madam Jiang, inside, heard her say softly, "I washed the rice for this porridge myself, and it's very clean. I don't know if your Second Master wants it salty or sweet, so I didn't buy any pickles." Hearing this, Madam Jiang knew the reason why the family was suddenly cooking porridge this afternoon. The elder daughter came back into the house, and Madam Jiang pretended not to know anything. She lit a lamp and put it on a table by the bedside kang, continuing to do her work. The elder daughter said, "Mom, you don't want to eat porridge, do you? I'll cook a bowl of noodles for you." Madam Jiang said, "Why are you making noodles when you've already cooked porridge?" The elder daughter said, "Because I know you don't like to drink millet porridge." Madam Jiang said, "Since you knew I didn't like to drink millet porridge, why did you cook such a big pot?" Saying this, she left the elder daughter speechless, only smiling faintly. She busily took the pot off the stove and put the stove back into the kang opening. She served two bowls of porridge and put a bowl of cold salted turnip shreds from the drawer on the table. Then she dragged a broken chair close to the table, picked up her chopsticks, and slowly chewed two turnip shreds in her mouth. Madam Jiang said, "You don't like to drink millet porridge either, do you? If you're cooking it for Second Master Gan, don't cook so much." The elder daughter lowered her head, held the porridge bowl to her lips, and slowly sipped it. Madam Jiang felt that these words might be somewhat embarrassing to her daughter, so she said, "The affairs of the world are truly hard to say. Wealthy families are tired of eating chicken, duck, fish, and meat, and want to drink millet porridge. We people who are tired of eating millet porridge can't even get a meal of dumplings." Just as she was saying this, she heard footsteps in the courtyard outside, and someone asked, "Who is it?" A man laughed and said, "It's me. I don't have anything to do. I've come to thank your family." After saying this, he left. This was Second Master Gan speaking. Madam Jiang laughed, "It's always like this. He shows up as soon as you mention him. Fortunately, we didn't say anything bad about Second Master, or there would have been trouble if he had heard it." The elder daughter said, "Second Master Gan isn't that kind of person. He wouldn't hold a grudge over small things." Madam Jiang, because her daughter was saying this, didn't argue with her. So, she didn't say anything more.

A Short Account of Watching the Sunrise on the Summit of Mount Tai 261

— Pingcao

Watching the sunrise on the summit of Mount Tai has long been a beautiful scene I've heard of; the actual experience of the sunrise at the summit of Tai is something I only experienced last year. In mid-September of autumn, a friend and I, after exerting ourselves for half a day, finally reached the summit at sunset. The desolation all around makes you suspect you've entered a dead town at the gates of hell. The piercingly cold wind carries with it a sharp whistling sound. Amidst the misty, undulating hills, a few vermilion pointed roofs of temples are revealed. The intermittent sound of temple bells tells you that there is still a kind of reclusive humanity on this mountain top.

We climbed towards that largest vermilion pointed roof for about another mile before reaching the side of that temple. Climbing a few stone steps, we could see the three large characters "Bixia Palace" on the wall of the gate tower. Looking inside, it was a deep, dark cavern. Deep inside, there was a light, a pale yellow light, illuminating an embroidered curtain, with golden figures of ox-headed monsters standing on both sides. Wisps of smoke floated from the incense burner. The threshold, pillars, and walls all revealed faint outlines. This was a sacred hall. Looking at this kind of eerie scene, we felt as if we were in the lair of mountain ghosts and spirits. A gust of cold wind blew, and we couldn't help but feel our hair stand on end, trembling with cold. Just as we were hesitating, a dog suddenly darted out from inside, barking a few times, followed by a monk who greeted us, and we slowly breathed a sigh of relief.

Because of the fatigue from climbing the mountain all day, we ate the vegetarian meal prepared by the monk, instructed him to wake us up tomorrow morning when it was time to see the sunrise, and then went to sleep hastily.

The next day, it wasn't even dawn when we both woke up. Without waiting for the monk to wake us, we got up and walked towards the Sun Viewing Pavilion. Clouds and snow were everywhere, and we couldn't see people on the opposite side. We climbed up along the stone path, and the strong wind made it difficult to breathe. Dark clouds were densely packed under our feet, and a few cold stars twinkled above our heads. Suddenly, a line of color appeared in the clouds in the east, slowly dyeing into a colorful glow. In the shimmering light of the glow, a red trace cracked open, growing larger and larger, and immediately turned into an arc shape. It jumped a few times, as if struggling, and then suddenly a full, huge crimson wheel jumped out. The red light below rose and fell suddenly, shaking for a while, and then slowly the colors faded. It is said that the red light is the seawater in the East Sea, and the sun emerges from the sea after bathing. This is certainly a mythological legend, but its clean and bright form is indeed very much like a passionate, just-bathed beauty.

As the crimson wheel rose, the clouds and mist gradually dissipated, only the wind was still blowing wildly as before. The stone tablet on the Sun Viewing Pavilion was faintly discernible. After touching and reading it, we learned that it was an imperial stele from the Qianlong period of the Qing Dynasty. Although the era was not far off, it was eroded by time, and ravaged by wind and rain, and most of the characters between the lines were no longer recognizable. We still returned along the same route, passed the Jade Emperor Peak, and viewed Li Si's Feng Chan Stele. The ancient sites near the Sun Viewing Pavilion, such as the Qingdi Palace, Yuanjun Palace, Dongyue Temple, Confucius Temple, Peach Blossom Cave, and Luban Cave, were all visited one by one. When we returned to Bixia Palace, the monk had already laid out the morning vegetarian meal. While eating, he talked a lot about the situation in the mountains. What made him most sigh was that in recent years, the number of people visiting the mountain had decreased, and the reduction in incense money for his temple was half of what it used to be, while the local government still levied incense donations on schedule. After giving the money for food and lodging, as we were about to leave, the sunlight was hanging on the treetop of an old pine tree in front of the palace.

Our officers and soldiers have long had the determination to never coexist with the Japanese bandits. However, the terrain in the Rehe area is vast, and the strength of one army cannot take care of the overall situation. We are very sad. I hope you will pay attention to our small sincerity. Kuiyuan, Commander of the 41st Army, bows. Yin Chen Yin, 7th Dispatch"

Xiong Xiling Talks About How Our Army Can Defend the Northern Mountains of the Great Wall After the Fall of Chengde 274

The Volunteer Army Consists Mostly of Cavalry, and Defending Dangerous Places is Not Their Strength

Subsequent Transportation is Convenient, Easy to Contact, and Can Be Defended for a Long Time

Since the fall of Chengde, eight or nine out of ten parts of Rehe Province have fallen into the hands of the enemy, causing a national shock. A reporter from the Xin Sheng News Agency specially visited Mr. Xiong BingSan at his residence this morning to inquire about the future of the situation in the north. Mr. Xiong replied as follows:

North China Can Still Be Supported 275

The stationed troops within the territory of Rehe are complicated, the command cannot be unified, and the transportation is extremely difficult. Its failure has been expected for a long time. However, the report that we will defend Gubeikou and Xifengkou is not accurate. The south of Chengde and Luanping, and the north of the Great Wall are all mountainous areas with very dangerous terrain, bordering Hebei Province. Transportation is more convenient, and the education and deployment of the troops are very different from those in Rehe Province. It is possible to defend it and not retreat to the mouths of the Great Wall, Xifeng, and Gubei.

The Volunteer Army is Mostly Cavalry 276

As for the saying that the Volunteer Army did not participate in the war, causing the fall of Chengde, it is far from the truth. However, the troops of the Volunteer Army Feng ZhanHai and Li HaiQing are mostly cavalry, and their function is to divide and harass. Now the Rehe war is to defend dangerous places and defend with trenches, which is the strength of the infantry, not the cavalry. Therefore, the effect is very small. Even Tang Yulin's troops are mostly cavalry, and their orders are not unified, and they have no training at all. Therefore, it is not enough to resist the Japanese bandits.

Our Army Lacks Artillery 277

In the Rehe war, in terms of military equipment, the enemy's strength is very different from ours, and we rely entirely on the terrain, just like the 19th Route Army's response to the war in Shanghai. The enemy attacked with planes and artillery, and we could not respond. We relied on trench warfare for infantry and cavalry charges, but the mountains are mostly stony and difficult to dig trenches. We used heavy artillery to defend, but our army lacked artillery, so it was difficult to defend.

The Volunteer Army Will Retreat to Chahar 278

In recent days, there have been many rumors that the Volunteer Army has retreated to Gubeikou, and General Zhu Ziqiao has been ordered to personally command, which is ridiculous. Because the Volunteer Army was previously stationed in the Kailu Suidong area, if Kailu and others are not defended, they will retreat to the vicinity of Chifeng. Now that Chengde has fallen, how can the Volunteer Army fly over the Japanese military garrison and go to Gubeikou? Those who know the situation in Rehe can see that it is absurd. The Volunteer Army can only retreat from the Linxi area to the Duolun area of Chahar Province. As for Mr. Xiong himself, he plans to return north within the second time.

Japanese Immigrants in Jilin 279

Among Them Are Veterans of the Russo-Japanese War

(Tokyo) Three hundred farmers who are preparing to establish an Osaka colony in the Jilin Jiaohua River basin at the beginning of April this year, of whom one hundred are currently considering the details of the colonial plan. Mr. Osaka Bandadao is the main initiator. US Gold Export Ban Impacts the Entire World 280

British Exchange Rates in a State of Near Shutdown

France Also Trending Towards Abandoning the Gold Standard

Japanese Stock Exchange Decides to Open Today

India's Purchasing Power Increases Demand for Silver in Our Country

Reuter's, London, 6th - A key figure in the London financial market commented on the impact of the US financial crisis, saying that the problem is extremely significant and that no one can answer it. Britain, apart from the US dollar, is currently conducting foreign exchange trading as usual, but transactions are limited. Generally, people want to wait and see how things develop. Some expect the situation to improve, and the appreciation of the pound is expected. However, efforts are currently being made to prevent the pound from rising too much.

Reuter's, London, 6th - The British government has not criticized the US financial crisis, but is observing the steps taken by the US to deal with its domestic difficulties with sympathetic attention. Banking circles in the Netherlands and France both expect the United States to abandon the gold standard, believing that this is the natural outcome of the financial crisis. Parisian bankers expect a large amount of French capital to be transferred from the United States back to France, as it is considered safer there. Italian financial circles regard the US ban as an unexpected move. The Roman market has now suspended foreign currency trading. Silver and gold brokers in Bombay expect demand for silver from China to increase and India's purchasing power to increase accordingly. Americans traveling in Cairo, Egypt, today could exchange one US dollar for 20 piastres, whereas on Friday one US dollar could be exchanged for 27 Egyptian piasters.

Reuter's, London, 6th - As European capitals speculate about the repercussions of the US banking crisis, a prominent Roman banker published an article stating that even if the United States abandons the gold standard, Italy will not. Opinions in Paris generally do not oppose France's ban on cash exports. The French newspaper "Debate" advises the Bank of France not to transport cash to countries that have abandoned a stable currency, and says that the British Exchange Equalisation Account will no longer be able to control the US dollar, and will now focus all its efforts on the franc and absorb the large amount of cash in France.

Denstu, Tokyo, 7th - Upon receiving news of the US ban on gold exports, Minister of Commerce and Industry Nakajima told reporters that the Japan-US exchange rate in the Japanese grey market had reached $26 USD, and it was expected to rise to $30 USD. As a result, imports and exports will inevitably be greatly affected. If the United States abandons the gold standard, Germany can be considered separately, but France will find it difficult to maintain the gold standard, as will the Netherlands. If the whole world bans gold exports, international trade will inevitably be placed on a special relationship. At present, we can only wait and see how the situation develops. The temporary implementation of a ban on gold exports may continue for a considerable period.

Denstu, Tokyo, 7th - Regarding the impact of the US financial panic on the Japanese textile industry, Seijiro Miyajima, President of Nisshin Spinning, said that although the Japanese textile industry has been greatly affected by the US ban on gold exports, there is no need to be pessimistic overall. The soaring Japanese yen and the falling price of cotton are indeed losses, but they are temporary and not significant. The sharp rise in the Japanese exchange rate is indeed sufficient to prevent exports, but the pound price of competing country Britain will inevitably rise, so there is no need to be pessimistic.

Japan League, Tokyo, 7th - After the US ban on gold exports was announced, private gold traders in Japan estimated that the US exchange rate would rise sharply. On the 6th, they planned to sell cash to the Bank of Japan. As a result of discussions yesterday afternoon between Vice Minister Kuroda of the Ministry of Finance and Director of the Finance Bureau Tomita, it was decided to consult with the Bank of Japan authorities on the 7th to stop the government from purchasing cash.

Havas, Paris, 6th - The US banking crisis has not had a significant impact in France. Among the currencies of various countries, only the French franc, the Dutch florin, and the Swiss franc can currently be exchanged for cash. In terms of finance, France has not had cash reserves in the United States for a long time, and France's trade with the United States was previously a surplus, but this is no longer the case. As for French people buying US securities, it is generally said that given the wealth of the United States, these securities will soon be able to recover their original value. Therefore, today the situation of the French stock exchange and various banks is still the same as before. Foreign rumors that the Bank of France is preparing to assist the US Federal Reserve Bank are actually inaccurate.

Havas, London, 6th - With the banking crisis in the United States, internationally, efforts are now being made to salvage the situation. Today, the Bank of England, the US Federal Reserve Bank, and the Bank of France exchanged information to consider the issue of the US dollar resuming pricing. However, the extent to which the US ban on gold exports will extend beyond what is expected, and whether the price of the US currency will fall as a result, is still unknown to the general public. Britain previously had a system for regulating exchange rates to prevent excessive fluctuations in the pound. After the US ban on gold exports, the regulatory fund must adapt to the new situation. Some people say that it is not appropriate for the pound to rise against the US exchange rate now, so they advocate stabilizing the pound price as soon as possible.

Havas, London, 6th - According to news from New York, the local stock exchange has decided to continue operations, and the opening time will be determined later. US bankers expect the authorities to use all kinds of methods to maintain the gold standard. The "Commercial Daily" reported that some financial officials in France, the Netherlands, Belgium, and Switzerland are prepared to help the United States maintain the gold standard.

Havas, London, 6th - At the close of the stock exchange, the pound rose slightly. The French exchange rate was 88 francs and 30 centimes. There was no market for the US exchange rate.

Denstu, Tokyo, 7th - Yesterday afternoon, the Ministry of Finance invited Vice President Fukai of the Bank of Japan and Director General Kodama of Yokohama Specie Bank to the Ministry of Finance to exchange views on the US financial panic. They all believed that the content of Roosevelt's countermeasures was not very clear, and it could not be determined whether it would develop into a suspension of the gold standard. It was unanimously advocated that we could only wait and see how the situation develops and then dispersed. These kinds of meetings will continue to be held in the future.

China League, Tokyo, 7th - The Nagoya Cotton Yarn Exchange held a meeting this morning and decided to open immediately. Upon hearing the news, the Tokyo Commodity Exchange also convened an emergency meeting. As a result of discussions, it was said that the impact was not significant, and it was decided to open. The situation after the opening was stable. The stock exchanges that have been suspended will open simultaneously tomorrow.

A Study of the Issue of Severing Diplomatic Relations with Japan 284

Opinions of a Certain Legal Expert

Seven Points Should Be Carefully Considered

Since the Japanese army invaded Rehe, there have been many calls from outside for severing diplomatic relations with Japan. On the 5th, a Central News Agency reporter specifically visited a certain legal expert to inquire about his opinions on severing diplomatic relations with Japan. He was kind enough to express his views from a legal perspective. The following is a summary:

The Consequences of Severing Diplomatic Relations 285

There are no clear provisions in international law regarding the legal consequences of severing diplomatic relations. Fauchillo's "Treatise on International Conventions: The Resolution of International Disputes" divides international disputes into two types: peaceful methods and coercive methods. Coercive methods can be further divided into retaliation, revenge, detention, severance of diplomatic relations, peacetime blockade, and other types. Fauchillo's writings state that [the severance of diplomatic relations between two countries due to one country destroying the other's property rights does not necessarily lead to a state of war between the two countries]. Hershcy's "International Law" states that the severance of diplomatic relations is a form of protest and is generally used to indicate an unusually tense relationship between the two countries. It may not be difficult to follow up with a war after the severance of diplomatic relations. Lawrence's "Principles of International Law" states that [a country may temporarily sever diplomatic relations with another country for major reasons. However, this kind of behavior is a significant insult and constitutes a sign of rupture, which is very close to a formal war and can actually lead to a formal war]. The opinions of the above-mentioned scholars differ. However, based on historical facts, the severance of diplomatic relations does not necessarily lead to war. The following are some examples: (1) In 1892, Greece and Romania severed diplomatic relations due to the Shi Bo Incident, but the two countries did not engage in war afterwards. (2) In 1903, several countries expressed dissatisfaction with the assassination of King Alexander and severed diplomatic relations with Serbia, but diplomatic relations were soon restored. (3) In 1906, France and Venezuela severed diplomatic relations. In 1913, the two countries signed a protocol to restore diplomatic relations. The protocol stipulated that various demands should be resolved by legal and arbitration methods. (4) During the European War, ten countries including Brussels and Bolivia were only in a state of neutral diplomatic relations with Germany and did not declare war.

The Methods of Severing Diplomatic Relations 286

There are various ways to terminate diplomatic relations. (1) Complete rupture, giving passports to the diplomatic representatives sent by the country with which diplomatic relations have been severed. (2) Notifying the government of the country concerned of the severance of diplomatic relations and recalling the ambassador to its own country. (3) Notifying the governments of related countries of the termination of diplomatic relations and recalling the minister to its own country. (4) Recalling the minister to its own country and embassy staff and notifying a third country to act on behalf of its interests. (5) Recalling the minister to its own country and leaving a certain member of the embassy to act on its behalf.

The Issue of Severing Diplomatic Relations 287

If China implements the severance of diplomatic relations with Japan, there are several issues that must be considered. (1) Japan's diplomatic representatives should be given passports and sent back to their country. However, if Japan's diplomatic representatives move to the Shanghai Concession and do not return to their country, putting us in a difficult position, what should we do? (2) After the severance of diplomatic relations, can Japan's concessions in China be taken back? Can all other treaty relations between China and Japan be abolished immediately? (3) If Japanese warships still sail in our territorial waters or dock at our ports, what methods can we use to stop and ban them? (4) Can the Japanese troops stationed in our territory be deported? (5) The severance of diplomatic relations cannot immediately be regarded as an act of hostility or the first step in a declaration of war. However, if the violent Japan is unreasonable and interprets it as such, uses it as an excuse, implements retaliation, withdraws overseas Chinese, and expands its aggression, how will we resist? Because in the League of Nations, we have promised not to take actions to expand the situation. However, if the League of Nations believes that it is an action to expand the situation after the severance of diplomatic relations, what will happen? Furthermore, if Japan or a member of the League of Nations Council or Committee raises the issue of the severance of diplomatic relations and says that it is a step towards engaging in war, will our country's position be affected? (7) It is said that if China wants to invoke Article 16 of the Covenant, it must first sever diplomatic relations with Japan. Otherwise, on the one hand, it wants to ask the powers to implement an economic blockade, while on the other hand, the two countries themselves are still holding friendly talks, which is very contradictory. However, after the severance of diplomatic relations, will various countries immediately be able to assist our country in invoking Article 16 of the Covenant? The above-mentioned issues are all issues that must be carefully considered before severing diplomatic relations with Japan. (Central News Agency)

He Yingqin Passes Through Jinan and Has a Candid Conversation with Han 288

Han Talks About the Peacefulness of the Shandong Coast

He Says He is Working Hard to Plan Resistance Against Japan

According to a person from Jinan, Minister of Military Administration He Yingqin and Minister of Interior Huang Shaoheng took a train north the other day. When they passed through Jinan, Governor of Shandong Province Han Fuqu, Director of the Department of Civil Affairs Li Shuchun, and Director of the Department of Education He Siyuan, etc., all went to the station to welcome them. He got off the train and shook hands with Han and others to exchange greetings. He then invited Han to board the train for a meeting. After boarding the train, He asked if any news from the front had been received here. Han replied that newspapers had reported that Chifeng and Lingyuan had been lost. He said that he had received a telegram from Yang Gengguang yesterday saying that Chifeng had not been lost and that Sun Dianying's army had arrived, but the situation was still critical. He also asked how the Shandong coast was. Han replied that it was still peaceful, but there was talk that Japanese women and children in Jinan were preparing to return to their country. Qingdao, Yantai, Longkou, and the Jiaoji Railway line were all fine. While they were talking, He received another telegram from Yang Jie saying that Lingyuan had been recaptured and that Sun Dianying's army in Chifeng was pursuing the enemy. Han said that the two ministers must have good plans for going north and that their strength could be equivalent to hundreds of thousands of soldiers. He replied that he would do his best to help Hanqing plan everything. In the future, Hanqing may have to go to the front line to command, and he would also have to ask Xiangfang (Han's character name) for help. Han said that national affairs were not a matter of helping each other. If it was necessary, he would go all out, but he did not want to be fragmented and divide his forces. He was willing to get 30,000 elite soldiers and take charge of one side alone. The supply of food and fodder to the hundreds of thousands of soldiers at the front was the most urgent matter, and the central government had to plan for this. He replied that plans had already been made. He had not been to Jinan for 20 years and saw that many chimneys had been added. He thought it had made great progress. Because when he came to Jinan in the second year of the Republic (1913), there was only one chimney in the electric light company. Han replied that there were now many small factories and three new spinning mills, so there was no need to use foreign goods in the future. He also said that the ministers had a major task. Otherwise, they could get off the train and stay for a while. He replied that when he returned to Beijing, he would get off the train and take a look. The Shandong coast was also very important, and Xiangfang's responsibility was also heavy. They had a candid conversation for about half an hour before Han took his leave and He and others continued north on the same train.

Including a Military Discussion Committee

and Six Specialized Committees

Guangzhou Communication: The Southwest National Defense Council has established various specialized committees. The organizational regulations are as follows: (Article 1) The specialized committees are organized in accordance with the provisions of Article 8 of the Organizational Regulations of the National Defense Council. (Article 2) The organization of the specialized committees is divided into the following types, all of which are subordinate to the National Defense Council: (1) Military Discussion Committee, (2) Weapons Specialized Committee, (3) Air Defense Specialized Committee, (4) Coastal Defense Specialized Committee, (5) Fort Specialized Committee, (6) Financial Specialized Committee, (7) Military Chemical Specialized Committee. (Article 3) Various specialized committees are convened temporarily by order of the National Defense Council. (Article 4) The convocation of a certain specialized committee in accordance with the provisions of Article 2 of these Regulations constitutes a certain committee. (Article 5) The Military Discussion Committee is organized by the following personnel: 1. Personnel with rich military knowledge and experience designated by the Southwest National Defense Council; 2. Senior military officers and senior staff officers of various provinces. 3. The Southwest National Defense Council. The Weapons Specialized Committee is composed of the following personnel: 1. Specialized personnel designated or hired by the Southwest National Defense Council; 2. Factory directors, deputy factory directors, or technicians of weapons manufacturing plants in various provinces; 3. Chiefs of staff and chiefs of ordnance departments of the highest military authorities in various provinces; 4. Fortress commanders of various provinces; 5. Directors and staff officers of the Southwest National Defense Council. (Article 7) The Air Defense Specialized Committee is organized by the following personnel: 1. Specialized personnel designated or hired by the Southwest National Defense Council; 2. Chiefs of staff of the highest military authorities in various provinces; 3. The highest air force officers in various provinces; 4. Directors of public security bureaus of the provincial capitals of various provinces; 5. Directors and staff officers of the Southwest National Defense Council. (Article 8) The Coastal Defense Specialized Committee is organized by the following personnel: 1. Specialized personnel designated or hired by the Southwest National Defense Council; 2. Chiefs of staff of the highest military authorities in various provinces; 3. The highest naval officers in various provinces; 4. Directors and staff officers of the Southwest National Defense Council. (Article 9) The Fort Specialized Committee is organized by the following personnel: 1. Specialized personnel designated or hired by the Southwest National Defense Council; 2. Chiefs of staff of the highest military authorities in various provinces; 3. The highest fortress officers in various provinces; 4. The highest naval officers in various provinces; 5. Directors and staff officers of the Southwest National Defense Council. (Article 10) The Financial Specialized Committee is organized by the following personnel: 1. Specialized personnel designated or hired by the Southwest National Defense Council; 2. Chiefs of the military supply departments of the highest military authorities in various provinces; 3. Directors of the finance departments of various provinces or their representatives; 4. Directors and staff officers of the Southwest.

National Defense Council. (Article 11) The Military Chemical Specialized Committee is organized by the following personnel: 1. Specialized personnel designated or hired by the Southwest National Defense Council; 2. Chiefs of staff of the highest military authorities in various provinces; 3. Factory directors or technicians of weapons manufacturing plants in various provinces; 4. Military chemistry instructors of military schools in various provinces; 5. Directors and staff officers of the Southwest National Defense Council. (Article 12) The chairman of the meetings of various specialized committees is rotated by the members of the National Defense Committee. However, in case of absence due to business, a temporary chairman may be elected from among the attending members. (Article 13) The secretary of the General Affairs Office of the National Defense Council is responsible for recording the minutes of the meetings of various specialized committees and compiling and distributing them to the members of the National Defense Committee and various specialized personnel. (Article 14) The meetings of various specialized committees are held within the National Defense Council. (Article 15) If there are any matters not covered in these regulations, they shall be amended by order of the National Defense Council. (March 1)

(2) The finance, education, construction, and public security bureaus under the county governments in Anhui Province were previously ordered by the provincial government to be changed to sections. To date, some have been reorganized in accordance with the order, some are still following the old system, and some have changed their names but the actual organization is no different from before. In order to facilitate administration, the provincial government should unify the organization. The provincial government's standing committee recently discussed and decided on the organizational principles of the county governments. Except for the education bureau, which will temporarily retain the old system due to historical reasons, and the finance bureau, which should be changed to a county finance committee in accordance with the regulations of the Three Provinces Bandit Suppression Headquarters, the remaining construction and public security bureaus will all be changed to sections and directly subordinate to the county government. At this moment, the provincial government has drafted the organizational regulations of the county government in accordance with the above-mentioned principles. Once the provincial government's standing committee passes them, they will be implemented separately. In addition, in order to understand the actual situation of county administration for assessment purposes, Director of the Department of Civil Affairs Luo Liangjian also plans to visit various counties in southern and central Anhui Province for a thorough inspection. The Gold Market Crisis is Gradually Stabilizing 292

The Market Situation Rose Slightly This Morning, Seeming to Have a Turning Point

Banking Circles Say Our Country Has Not Been Affected

According to the Central News Agency, the financial crisis in the United States, coupled with rumors of the abolition of the gold standard, has had a severe impact on the financial markets of various countries. The financial market in this city was also affected yesterday, with the price of gold plummeting and people's hearts shaken. As of this noon, the decline has not slowed down slightly. This morning's market situation opened at 682 taels, then fell sharply to 677 taels. Then, due to news that the United States was maintaining the gold standard, it gradually turned around and rose to 692 taels. Looking at the market situation this morning, the ups and downs in an instant reached a difference of more than ten taels, which is indeed an unprecedented change in the financial world. It is expected that there will still be drastic changes in the afternoon. The reporter of China Central News Agency revisited a senior official in the banking world this morning and asked whether the US order banning cash exports would affect the banking world in our country. According to the answer, US President Roosevelt ordered a ban on cash exports and announced that various banks would suspend operations for several days in order to resolve the financial crisis during this period. The ban on cash exports has absolutely no impact on the country, and it is predicted that the sharp drop in the price of gold will be very short-lived.

According to New Voice News Agency, yesterday's sharp drop in the price of gold was due to the fact that the US exchange rate was priceless and the gold market could not open, which led to inquiries to the gold trading industry. Therefore, the gold trading exchange held a meeting all night yesterday to discuss solutions. Fortunately, this morning's gold market opened at 82 taels, the lowest was 76 taels, and the closing price was 92 taels. The crisis seems to have subsided.

Entire Communication in Rehe Suspended　The Shanghai Postal Administration's Parcel Office has already announced the suspension of accepting parcels for Rehe since yesterday morning. As of 8:00 AM this morning, the Shanghai Bureau Management Office issued a formal notice to temporarily suspend the acceptance of ordinary letters and parcels destined for Rehe Province. All subordinate branches were instructed to comply. The notice stated: "To whom it may concern, we hereby relay Postal General Bureau torpedo number 84. We hereby inform you for your information and compliance. Mail Management Office, March 7th.

Postal Workers Advance and Retreat with the Troops　According to a statement from a General Bureau official, the Tianjin Postal Bureau has not yet provided any reports regarding postal services in Rehe. According to an official at the Telegraph Bureau, telegrams to the Northeast regions were still being accepted and dispatched by the bureau last week, but very few were able to reach their destination, and some could not be delivered at all. Only yesterday afternoon (March 6th) did the Ministry of Communications send a telegram instructing that telegrams to Rehe, Heilongjiang, Liaoning, and Jilin be temporarily suspended from acceptance and dispatch. Therefore, the bureau has officially ceased accepting telegrams to the aforementioned regions starting today.

Around 9:30 AM this morning, a large number of Japanese marines, accompanied by groups of three to five Japanese residents, were making a show of force on the streets of North Sichuan Road in Hongkou. Fortunately, no accidents occurred. According to the Japanese-language Shanghai Daily News today, the Special Naval Landing Force conducted combat training at the Hongkou New Park, the Volunteer Corps shooting range, and the area near Jiangwan Road from 7:00 AM this morning to boost the morale of the marines. Commander Sugisaka served as the general supervisor, and Captain Kawashima, commander of the First Battalion, served as the commander of the Red Army, leading armored vehicles and half of the First Battalion, along with the Headquarters Command Company, to set up solid defensive positions in several locations near the New Park. The Green Army, the attacking force, was commanded by Major Futada, commander of the Second Battalion, who led the Second Battalion's tank and artillery units to rapidly advance from the western Shuishui area towards the Red Army's positions, launching a fierce attack. They planned to seize the defensive positions in one fell swoop at dawn. At the same time, the two armies engaged in hand-to-hand combat, with the elite troops of the Green Army and the iron-blooded troops of the Red Army engaging in a fierce mock battle.

Stole Older Brother's Handgun for a Friend 302

Liu Peide Was Young and Inexperienced

Xu Fengbin Was Daring and Reckless

Zhang Jinhai and Xu Fengbin, natives of Tongzhou, were unemployed and staying at room 132 of the Hongyun Hotel at number 1009 Hainin Road. They had pawned all their clothes and were unable to make a living. A Cantonese friend, Liu Peide, 16 years old, was studying at a certain school and lived at number 77, Tongchangli, on the same road. (His older brother, Liu Ruoqun, was a special constable and carried a handgun.) Liu visited the hotel and Zhang and Xu asked for his help, saying they were penniless and it was difficult to make it. They claimed there was an opportunity to get money but they didn't have a handgun to accomplish their goal. Zhang Juryong, a native of Zhenjiang, opened a flower gambling den at number 318 nearby and was making good money. If Liu had a handgun, they could impersonate police officers and borrow dozens of silver dollars from him. They asked if Liu could borrow a handgun and begged him to help. Liu readily agreed. He returned home while his brother was out, found the key hidden in the drawer where the handgun was kept, and took it. He carried it with him and went to the hotel again at [divination] time yesterday morning. He showed them the handgun and said it was ready to go. Zhang and Xu were overjoyed and went to Zhang Juryong's house and falsely claimed they were there to catch gamblers. They pointed to Liu Peide and claimed he was an investigator from the HSBC police and that if they paid ten silver dollars, they would be fine. Zhang Juryong panicked and gave Xu a cloth coat to pawn. Xu went to the Shunli Pawnshop near the North Jiangxi Road and Laobazi Road and got only six silver dollars. He gave Zhang Juryong a pawn ticket and one silver dollar and asked Zhang Juryong to make up the remaining money. They agreed on a date to pay. Liu and the other two returned to the hotel and Zhang Juryong secretly reported it to the Hongkou police, accusing them of extortion and intimidation, practically robbery. Detectives Zhang Faxiang and Wang Runhe secretly went to the hotel and arrested Liu and the other two. They found five silver dollars on Xu. They were taken into custody along with Tao Xiaohai, a native of Tongzhou who was also suspected. Upon questioning, Liu said the handgun was at his home in the drawer and locked. The detectives went to his brother and explained the case. They took the handgun as evidence. This morning, they were sent to the Third Criminal Court of the First Special District Court. Police lawyer Zhang Tianyin detailed the case and stated that Liu Peide's brother was completely unaware that his brother had stolen the handgun. The police did not prosecute him and the handgun was returned to him. Zhang Hua, the wife of Zhang Juryong, testified. Liu Peide said the handgun was his brother's and that Xu and Zhang asked him for help. He did not receive any money. Lawyer Ye Shaoying defended him. Xu and Zhang claimed that because the plaintiff opened a flower gambling den and a large gambling den, they were destitute and borrowed money from him. The court ordered them to be remanded in custody and set a date for sentencing. Tao Xiaohai was released.

Verdicts Delivered Separately This Morning in the Kidnapping Case of Sun Yangru 303

Three Convicts Sentenced to Death

Other Sentences Varied

Sun Yangru, a 47-year-old native of Anhui, served as the manager of Tongfeng Company at number 25 Renji Road. On December 4th of last year, at 4:00 PM, Sun was driving his private car to visit a friend at number 67 Xieqiao Road, Jing'an Temple Road, when he was suddenly met by several kidnappers armed with weapons, who kidnapped Sun and demanded a large ransom. Sun's family, after Sun was kidnapped, proceeded with the procedures for preparing the ransom for his release, without reporting to the police. Subsequently, Lu Liankui, Chief Detective of the General Investigation Division of the Public Concession Police, received a report from an informant and immediately began an investigation. As a result, the location of the hostage was discovered. He supervised detectives Liu Shaokui, Feng Zhiming, Shao Jingfan, etc., and rescued Sun safely at a foreign house number 5, Yideli, Raul Road in the French Concession. At that time, the kidnappers Lu Ge and Wang Yaohua tried to escape over the roof. Lu fell to the ground and died on the spot, and Wang was seriously injured and arrested. Subsequently, the kidnappers Yang Baofu, Tang Jinsheng, Ma Lisang, Gao Shanqing, Wang Weichuan, Wu Anwen, Guo Yusheng, Wang Chunshan, Jia Jinshan, Wang Jingtang (former captain of the Municipal Public Security Bureau's Water Patrol Team), Li Xitang (Sun Yangru's brother-in-law), Chen Chenshuo (director of the Jiangdu Poor Children's Home), women Wu Wangshi and Wang Dingshi were arrested one after another. A handgun, more than 30 bullets, and a car number 6335 used for kidnapping were confiscated. Wang Jingtang's private car number 11624 was also confiscated. Police lawyer Ru Baoyi filed a public prosecution with the First Special Court in accordance with the Regulations on the Punishment of Bandits. The Special Court repeatedly interrogated and concluded the case. The details have been published in this newspaper. This morning, Qian Hongye, President of the Criminal Tribunal, ascended to the Criminal Tribunal One and announced the verdicts. Yang Baofu, Tang Jinsheng, and Wang Yaohua were each sentenced to death. Ma Lisang, Gao Shanqing, and Wu Anwen were each sentenced to life imprisonment, and each was deprived of their civil rights for life. Guo Yusheng and Wang Chunshan were each sentenced to fifteen years of imprisonment. Wang Weichuan, Jia Jinshan, and Chen Chenshuo were each sentenced to seven years of imprisonment. For all defendants other than those sentenced to death or life imprisonment, the number of days detained before the determination of the judgment was offset against the imprisonment by two days for one day of imprisonment. Wu Wangshi, Wang Dingshi, and Li Xitang were all found not guilty. The handgun, bullets, and car number 6335 were all confiscated. After the verdict, the court adjourned.

Talking Points

Injustice for Tang Yulin 吾 305

"Chengde Falls, Tang Yulin Flees Without Fighting" Such large headline characters stabbed into our eyes in the newspaper. Which patriotic person did not beat their chest and stomp their feet? Who didn't want to grab him and tear him into pieces? Even Comrade Zhang, famous throughout the world for his "non-resistance policy", couldn't help but thunder and "order the arrest of Tang Yulin, and if caught, he will be executed to uphold the law of the land". How righteous, how grand, how just. Therefore, we ordinary people cannot help but believe that Young Marshal Zhang is indeed a "vanguard against Japan", indeed a "pillar of the nation", and we cannot help but "tighten our belts and economize", "destroy our homes to relieve the nation's difficulties", and diligently wire one ten-thousandth of our property to Prince Shuncheng's mansion, begging him to sacrifice himself for the country. From then on, accumulating little by little will lead to success in resisting Japan. There is great hope. In the future, there is even the possibility of doing cigarette advertising.

The old rascal Tang Yulin also found out that as long as he "declared" resistance against Japan, he would have money coming in. So, after being a prince and minister under the reign of Xuantong for more than a year, he also said that he would "fight to the end". But the Japanese imperialists refused to let him play both sides, and the old running dog was naturally unwilling to make it real. So, after thinking for a moment, a plan came to him. He immediately packed his belongings, loaded them on a car, and the so-called "fleeing without fighting" in the newspaper was actually a donation to the master.

From this point of view, his "declaration of resistance" and "fleeing without fighting" were clearly planned in the great plan of saving the country. The painted face takes one step forward, and the small painted face takes two steps back. They had already discussed it clearly behind the stage. Moreover, he is the direct successor of the "non-resistance policy", so of course he has to abide by the family tradition. However, the people of the country cannot forgive him, and they scold the wooden puppet instead of the one pulling the strings. Comrade Zhang can give the three northeastern provinces to his grandfather as a gift and become an important figure in the party and state, while Tang Yulin is only imitating his predecessors by giving away one province, and he is to be "arrested" and "executed". How very very much indeed.

However, Tang Yulin's deserving to die is beyond doubt. Moreover, Comrade Zhang also said that he should be shot after questioning his conscience. Therefore, his heinous crime is imaginable. At the same time, we have now learned another serious lesson: to beg these warlord grandpas to resist imperialism for us is like inviting a thief to guard against thieves. Moreover, in order to thoroughly resist imperialism, we must use the power of our masses to completely eliminate these dogs, and then we can achieve the final victory in the anti-imperialist national revolutionary war.

Science

Artificial Lacquer Oil Varnish 307

— Leng Mei

Previously, I saw an article about "Natural Lacquer" in this publication, which reminded me of this important "Artificial Lacquer." The main raw material for artificial lacquer is tung oil. Before tung oil was imported, European and American countries used linseed oil as raw material, but its products were less durable and did not dry as easily as artificial lacquer made from tung oil. Artificial lacquer made from tung oil is of good quality, very durable and easy to dry, and waterproof. It is comparable to natural lacquer.

(1) Types 丨 There are many types of artificial lacquer. Generally, they can be divided into three types: (A) Positive Artificial Lacquer "Long oil" Varnish, which contains more tung oil. (B) Neutral Artificial Lacquer "Medium Oill" Varnish, which contains a moderate amount of tung oil. (C) Negative Artificial Lacquer "Short Oil Varnish, which contains less tung oil. The above three types have their own special uses. Positive artificial lacquer is for outdoor use. Neutral artificial lacquer is for flooring. Negative artificial lacquer is for indoor use.

(2) Raw Materials 丨 The raw material ratios for positive, neutral, and negative artificial lacquers are as follows:

A. Positive Artificial Lacquer

Resin 100 pounds (If rosin is used, 10 pounds of lime must be added.)

Tung oil 35 gallons

Copper acetate 3.5 pounds

Acetic acid 1 pound

Turpentine or mineral oil 50 gallons

B. Neutral Artificial Lacquer

Resin 100 pounds

Tung oil 18 gallons

Lead acetate 2 pounds

Cobalt acetate 0.5 pounds

Turpentine 33 gallons

C. Negative Artificial Lacquer

Resin 100 pounds

Tung oil 12 gallons

Lead acetate 1 pound

Cobalt acetate 0.25 pounds

Turpentine 27 gallons

Tung oil and resin are the main raw materials for artificial lacquer, and lead acetate and cobalt acetate are drying agents. Turpentine or mineral oil is a thinning agent.

(3) Equipment 丨 Only two things are needed: a lacquer pot and a resin tank. The lacquer pot should be made of iron, with a capacity of about 100 gallons. The bottom of the pot should be equipped with adjustable moving wheels. The resin tank is made of tung wood, 3 feet high and 1.5 feet in diameter.

(4) Manufacturing 丨 First, dissolve the resin (its melting point should be below 400 degrees Fahrenheit), and place it in the lacquer pot with tung oil. Heat it with a fierce fire to 500 degrees, maintain it for several hours, and wait until a suitable degree of solidification is obtained before extinguishing the fire. When the temperature drops to 300 degrees, add thinning agents such as turpentine to thin it.

If the melting point of the resin exceeds 400 degrees, the resin must first be dissolved with a small amount of tung oil in the resin tank, and then mixed with the remaining tung oil. This oil must also be burned to 500 degrees first.

(5) Inspection 丨 To inspect the quality of artificial lacquer, place a small drop of lacquer on a glass slide. If it appears transparent, it shows that the tung oil and resin are completely combined. Extend it with a finger to form a line. This line should be about 1 foot long. The best ones can be extended to 2 or 3 feet.

The New People in the Pavilion 308

— Ke Fu

The second landlord's pavilion room was empty and rented to a university graduate, who, in addition to having a diploma but no job, also had a wife as beautiful as a flower. Their renting the house broke Shanghai's record: renting for half a month.

This was also due to the kindness of the compassionate second landlady, because this handsome man in a Western suit said:

"······I want to find a job in Shanghai. If there is no hope in another half month, we will go home, so I only want to rent for half a month!"

"Yes! People who go out always have difficulties; then let's do this. The rent is seven yuan a month, and half a month will be four yuan!"

"······" He then took out a silver dollar.

They moved in that afternoon. This was a scholar's wife, a red-dressed girl in the most fashionable style in Shanghai!

It was night, and the pavilion room was filled with teasing laughter.

"Sir! This is······" the second landlord pushed open the pavilion door and asked.

"Her? She is my wife!"

"Oh! That's great! Sir, when you go to sleep, please turn off the light!" "Understood!" He said, "Sit down for a while!" The second landlady then retreated and said, "No! You enjoy yourselves!"

The next morning, the red-dressed girl left and did not return at night. The scholar was upstairs cooking on a gasoline lamp.

"Sir! Why hasn't your young mistress come back even at this time today?" The second landlord pushed in again and asked.

"Oh! She! She is studying at XX Middle School and is staying at the school tonight!" The scholar said.

"Oh! So that's how it is!"

"·················"

"Truly new people!" The second landlady retreated and went downstairs muttering to herself.

The Art of Getting Along in School 309

— Man

A few days ago, I saw "The Art of Getting Along" in your publication. We young people in school can't help but be eager to talk about our "art of getting along" in school. "Wide social connections" can be regarded as the sacred and inviolable truth of the art of getting along in our school: that is, you must be close to all three levels of teachers (upper level: such as the principal, the director of student affairs, and your own teaching teachers, etc. middle level: such as sports instructors. lower level: such as clerks and accountants, etc.) and three levels of students (upper level: those athletes who look like Red Indians, black faces, and wearing lantern pants. middle level: those bookworms who stay at home and get first place. lower level: the ghosts in the lower grades) up to the tea room in the school and the proprietress of those small shops outside, you have to be close to them all; as for the methods of getting close, they are nothing more than the three highest arts of getting along: "wind", "horse", and "cattle". For example: if you want to get close to those teachers, you have to invite them to a feast, or send them a few silver shields; if that teacher likes to smoke, you have to buy a few cans of Three-Five brand, or at least Cavenders. In short, you have to take advantage of every opportunity to send them what they like. If you want to get close to those athletes, you have to wear the same red hats and lantern pants as them. If you feel that your face is not black, you can grab a handful of mud and smear it on your face; ask for a few boxes of Beauty brand cigarettes in your spare time, or add a few dishes. As for getting close to those hard-working students, (most of the hard-working students are poor) you have to exaggerate, for example, if your surname is Jiang, you say that Chairman Chiang is your uncle, if it doesn't look like it, at least you must say that he is from my family, and you can find them a job after graduation, at least as a county magistrate, and they will naturally be close to you unconditionally. Also, if you have a skill, you must show it off greatly. For example, if you can play football, you have to put on your football shoes and kick a few times on the playground. If you can give a speech, you often have to show off your eloquence. Or if you can write some great works, you have to prepare a wall newspaper. If you can't do any of these things, and you only know how to eat, you must eat seven or eight bowls at every meal, even if your stomach is so full that it is about to burst, you still have to get the reputation of "King of Eating" and get everyone to pay attention to you.

If you do this after "wide social connections", the benefits are self-evident; for example, after you are close to those teachers, when you don't do well on the big exam, they will always give you a 70; if you hate the food in the dining hall and smash a few bowls in anger, of course the student affairs teacher will not see it and record a demerit. Being close to the sports instructor can also give you the opportunity to play a certain ball or be on a certain team to show off. Being close to the red-hatted ones allows you to fight with people and show off your power. Being close to the bookworms allows you to ask them to Pass during the exam while you can go to sleep. Being close to the little ghosts allows you to ask them to do things for you, and being close to the proprietress allows you to pay a few less yuan during the holidays······

In short, people who understand the art of getting along in school can be big shots and beat people······People who don't understand the art of getting along in school can only be little ghosts.

Communication from Shop Employees

Great Difficulty Ahead 312

— Pan Minshen

Editor Sir:

My cousin, Miss Mou, is not yet twenty years old, and a young widow. She has no children. Besides her parents-in-law, she also has three uncles-in-law. Her husband's family is well-off, but they have not yet divided the property. The wives of the brothers-in-law do not get along well, and there is a strong desire to live separately. Now that her parents-in-law are alive, they can still barely maintain the situation, but once the two elders pass away, she will have no support at all. Her maternal family is not wealthy either, truly a situation of bleak prospects and great difficulty ahead. From the perspective of modern people, in such a situation, of course, remarriage would be the proper course. However, those around her, and she herself, have all been washed by the old moral teachings, so she would never even think of the word "remarriage." One cannot deprive a common person of their will, and others cannot even broach the subject. Now, because she thinks about the darkness of the future, she frowns all day long, her beautiful face fading. As her close relative, I really feel I cannot stand by and do nothing. I ask, does a widow have the right to demand a division of her in-laws' property? Her dowry jewelry is now in the hands of her in-laws. Can she demand its return? Sir, the above questions seem to be outside the scope of "Communication from Shop Employees," but I am indeed a shop employee! Please give me a reply. (The following omitted) Sincerely, Pan Minshen.

XXXX

Editor's Note: What distinguishes humans from animals is that they need to live a spiritual life. A person cannot feel satisfied with material enjoyment alone; they also need spiritual comfort. Pan's cousin's husband is dead, and the love of a couple and the joy of companionship are of course hopeless. And because she has no children, she cannot, like other widows, transfer all her energy to maternal love. In this situation, even if her material aspects have been adequately resolved, we cannot help but advise her to remarry, especially since she faces great difficulty ahead! Therefore, we still advise Pan to persuade her to remarry. One cannot deprive a common person of their will, which is certainly true; however, the degree of persuasion has not yet reached the level of coercion, so there is no question of depriving her of her will! Why can't you broach the subject?

Current laws stipulate that children may not demand the division of parental property, but exceptions are allowed in special circumstances. For example, "If a widow and her in-laws, or a legitimate child and his stepmother, have become estranged and it is difficult to force them to live together, they may be allowed to divide the property and live separately." It seems that Pan's cousin's relationship with her in-laws has not yet reached the point of "estrangement and difficulty in forcing them to live together." However, if there is concrete evidence between her uncles-in-law and brothers-in-law's wives that is sufficient to prove the urgent need to secure future livelihood, they can also file a request for property division. As for the dowry jewelry, it is her private property and she absolutely has the right to demand its return.

Fiction

Coal Mountain (Continued) 313

— By Ep Falkowski, Translated by Zhixiang

VI

But now, after the outbreak of fuel competition in New Newland, New York, and other central markets selling hard coal, the impact was immediate. Hard coal mines were only working three or four days a week. Coal washing plants and open-pit mines were shut down, and machines were idle. Many workers felt that the current situation was not even as good as picking coal, chopping firewood, and transporting coal.

At the same time, managers and superiors became increasingly harsh and arrogant. New orders were issued daily from the head office in Pottsville, such as layoffs, reductions in timber, implementation of "dead work" (working without pay), and previously unenforced rules were now strictly enforced, such as smoking, taking leave the day after receiving wages, or arguing with the foreman, all of which were grounds for dismissal.

The cry of "cheap coal" was widespread. "We must now compete with kerosene and soft coal," the managers said. "Miners must cooperate with us to overcome this competition and restore our lost markets. This is our common struggle - it requires us to implement the "cooperation and efficiency" policy stipulated in the contract - each person contributing their part to save the hard coal industry..."

Meetings were being held in many coal-selling cities: managers of mines from various regions and representatives of labor unions were in attendance, all agreeing to reduce mine operating costs. They wore high collars, wide bow ties, and formal attire, indicating their hostility towards living in hotels: they spoke fluently, predicting that the long-awaited peace would restore the prestige of hard coal. Mine managers argued: "We must not strike again, we must defend our markets - workers and company employees must all pay attention to the common good."

After listening to these words, the labor union representatives - of humble origins and still retaining their lowliness - replied firmly and slyly, "The entire industry seems somewhat dubious."
