Film Special

American Garbo 314

— Cao

The throne has been seized, Greta Garbo should hurry back!

When Greta Garbo first returned to Sweden, who in Hollywood had heard the name Katharine Hepburn? Before "A Bill of Divorcement" was officially released, Americans had anticipated such a great "new discovery"; now that "A Bill of Divorcement" has been selected as one of the ten greatest films, and Katharine Hepburn's achievements are on par with John Barrymore at the forefront of honor, who doesn't know about this new discovery, "American Garbo" Katharine Hepburn?

This nickname was obtained in this way: when "A Bill of Divorcement" was screened, those who saw her high cheekbones and emotional face looked as if they were made from the same mold as the departed Garbo; at the same time,

She also possessed mystery, fearing to speak and even more fearing the pursuit of audiences. Therefore, the neurotic journalists, like discovering a new continent for the motherland, proclaimed that they had discovered a domestic Garbo!

In fact, she fears to speak not only in crowds. On her first day in Hollywood, this new mysterious woman, like Garbo, evaded camera shots in every possible way under the pursuit of film reporters. Even the publicity department of RKO could not obtain any information to promote her. It was only from other sources that they learned that she was twenty-four years old and the daughter of a wealthy family.

The reason why Greta Garbo is called mysterious is because she refuses to disclose anything about herself. Now, Garbo's "mysterious" throne has been seized by her. However, this young, light brown-haired girl has created her own seat. As the December issue of Motion Picture magazine praised her when it nominated her as a star:

We believe she is a great star –

Because she is the loyal model for a 1933 star - young, talented and experienced, and possessing a brilliant personality. Because she is a descendant of the wealthy, acting is her hobby, not a necessity. Because she is a gentle woman never seen on screen. Because she has received stage training and the highest level of education. Because she is "creative" and does not imitate the appearance of anyone on screen.

American Garbo Katharine Hepburn in a glimpse of her performance in "A Bill of Divorcement"

Audience Opinions

Review of "Spring Breeze and Willow Branches" 315

— Yu Hong

In this universe where money is almighty, even so-called sacred male-female "love", although said to be unconditional and without purpose, cannot escape the scope of money. However, is money sufficient to maintain eternal love? This is a question. "Spring Breeze and Willow Branches" is based on this point. It tells the story of a woman who is superstitious about money, taking money as the goal of love, changing her husband three times, abandoning her children twice, and finally ending up without a master, like willow branches broken in the spring breeze. Its intention and material are commendable. However, the facts are too clever and too hypocritical, with places where it is impossible for the facts to be,

The expressions are very stiff. Sang Xiuying, who plays the creditor, is simply acting like a puppet of the director. However, Chao Langen, although a comical supporting character, is still commendable. The language is also far-fetched. Except for Yang Naimei, they all curl their tongues and speak stiffly. The setting for the graduation ceremony at the university is also too simple.

Finally, regarding the pronunciation issue, because this is the result of preference, we cannot be satisfied with this and hope that Mr. Zhu Qingxian will continue to work hard and eventually surpass imported products.

My Criticism of "Torrent" 316

— Hong

The sensational "Torrent" has finally met with us. It uses a realistic theme, using the great floods in various provinces of China in the previous year as the background of the depiction, writing about the oppression of the peasant masses and the evils of the local bullies. However, we feel that the screenwriter has forcibly inserted such a love story into "Torrent," which is really unnecessary. Because in this way, not only does it reduce the power of "Torrent," but it also makes people doubt the reality of this story.

Although the director used many new techniques in "Torrent," it is a pity that he quietly let go of several places that should have been heavily depicted; although the scenes of the flood were edited very well, there were still too many. The interlude of the dance hall seems a bit like adding legs to a snake.

Among the characters in "Torrent," Gong Jianong's Liu Tiesheng is successful. Xia Peizhen's Suzhen, only when she tells Fu Xiujuan the story of Liu Tiesheng taking her in, are a few of the shots done best. Hu Die's Fu Xiujuan is very good in the first half, but the expressions in the second half are a bit too much. Wang Xianzai's Li Heqing, although not as fiery as Tan Zhiyuan's Fu Boren, is still very good.

Japanese Film Industry 317

— Zhao Peng

Japanese film companies are all subsidized with huge sums of money by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs. The films they shoot are like the following types: (1) Films that show the dignity of the nation, such as Japanese air force teams, Japanese marines, naval warships, naval exercises, etc. These all show the strength and majesty of their country. (2) Films of civil life, such as Japanese current industrial factories, education, sports, etc., all show the development of various industries in their country. (3) International films. These films are the most hateful. They sent many photographers to China, secretly filming the scenery and terrain of various places. They deliberately hired many actors to play out many internal war situations in China, and compiled them into English and French! They were sent to countries around the world, implying that China is an unorganized country. When the League of Nations investigation team passed through Japan, they specially filmed many films of Japanese civil and military officials receiving the investigation team, so that various countries showed considerable goodwill towards them. Other projects such as the Manchurian state, they have all filmed and broadcast to various countries. In addition to the above types of films, films about love, society, news, etc., must undergo strict inspection and banning by government agencies. In summary, all kinds of Japanese films contain propaganda components.

New Box Office Record in the United States 318

— Xin

The global recession may be the main reason why American movies cannot create new box office records. Since the record of "Cavalcade" at the Roxy was established, it has been proudly unshaken for two years, until recently, when it was broken by "State Fair." "State Fair" is a film that Fox has painstakingly produced for a year, because MGM filmed "Grand Hotel" and it caused a sensation. So Fox also gathered all the famous stars of the company, such as Janet Gaynor and Will Rogers, and spent 1.5 million dollars to make a better film. Now their goal has been achieved. The box office of "State Fair" in the first five days of its initial release reached 115,822 people, exceeding the record of "Cavalcade" by more than 5,000 people.

A Bunch of Film News 319

— Songfu

According to reliable sources, Chiang Kai-shek intends to shoot an unprecedented military film, which is currently being prepared. The deadline is tentatively set for one year, and the cost is estimated at around 100,000 yuan.

The scenes of Lianhua's new film "New Year's Eve" that had not been filmed, because Liu Jiqun has returned to Shanghai from the capital, the shots that Liu will shoot have been completed, and now it is all finished.

Seeing that Lianhua Company has published "Lianhua Pictorial," in order not to fall behind and to expand publicity, Mingxing Company will issue a "Mingxing Monthly" at the beginning of next month. Currently, articles are being solicited from male and female stars and employees of the company.

Since the success of "City Nights," Fei Mu is now living in Tianjin. It is said that he has been actively writing a moral tragedy recently, tentatively named "Wet Nurse." The majority has been completed and filming is expected to begin soon.

Bu Wancang of Lianhua First Factory will direct a film called "Light of Motherhood." Zhu Qingxian will be responsible for the sound part of this film, and the contract has been signed.

It is said that the wild child Wang Renmei will leave the Mingyue Opera Company and officially join Lianhua. A long-term contract is said to have been signed.

Someone Follows in Charlie Chaplin's Footsteps 320

— Luo Xiu

Nils Asther recently had a dispute with his wife Vivian Duncan over the future custody of their beloved daughter, which led to a lawsuit in court and a divorce was declared. However, the result was a victory for Vivian, who obtained custody of the girl.

Having failed, Niels followed in Charlie Chaplin's footsteps and asked the court to amend two points. First, the child may not leave Los Angeles without the permission of the parents and the court. Second, the child may not be involved in the film industry or on stage until the age of thirteen.

Unfortunately, both of these requests were rejected by the judge for trial.

New Plans of the Hehe Company 321

— Zong

"Spring Breeze and Willow Branches" has been released at the Beijing Grand Theater, and the sales record has exceeded the ideals of Wang Fuqing and Zhu Qingxian. Therefore, Wang Zhu, etc. have been preparing for the second sound film. According to the most reliable news, Zhu Qingxian's Hehe Company will implement his Qingxian-style sound film within this month. The script has been selected, the name of the play is "Roar," and the Western stage play "Fatherland" is used as the blueprint. He also wants to recruit several directors in Shanghai to form an editorial committee on a friendly basis. The editorial committee will be established within the 15th, and "Roar" will be prepared properly within the 25th, and filming will start before the end of the month at the latest.

Film Novel

Rasputin (10) 322

— Shi

She understood - all hope was extinguished. Suddenly, Neitaga walked into the room, whispering quietly, and said to her: "Your Majesty, God will never let him die!"

The Queen held her hand, begging: "Neitaga, please say it again! Only you give me hope!"

Neitaga held her for a moment, then whispered:

"Your Majesty, I have invited Rasputin… He is waiting outside. He can save him.”

“Rasputin!" The name was uttered in a quivering gasp. Even the Queen had heard the rebellious reports about this man and was afraid. But now, nothing else mattered. "Bring him in quickly," she said softly:

"Let me pray for the little prince." Rasputin said as he walked in, and the Queen felt all hope had vanished again.

"Clergymen all over the country are praying - none can save him!" She protested.

"I am not a clergyman, girl," Rasputin said solemnly: "I am an ordinary man, a man who believes deeply that God will answer your sincere request."

"We are grateful for anyone's prayers..." The Queen smiled bitterly, her hand making a gesture to ask him to leave. "Please go to the church to pray. They are all over there."

"God is not only in the church," Rasputin said slowly: "The sincere request of an ordinary man can move God more than all the hymns and recitations in the world. Only if you truly believe!"

"I truly believe!" The Queen said urgently: The mysterious power of this man had touched her.

"You do not truly believe, otherwise your hand would not be trembling like this!" Rasputin smiled benevolently. "And your tears would not be so contained in your eyes… If you truly believed like a child, then you would say: My son will be healed, because you are sent by God.”

"You are sent by God," the Queen said slowly, following his words:

"Now I will go see him," Rasputin suddenly became very mysterious: his arm raised, his voice becoming joyous. "Your son will live," he shouted.

"My son will live…" The Queen seemed to have been entranced by him, and walked along, shouting.
